Given the special situation today, however, the Ghost Scorpion clearly wouldn't listen to them.

"Master Ghost Scorpion, I think we could work something out. The price can be negotiated," one of the mice said.

The Ear Mice appeared to be very generous, and there were no doubts about their powerful financial capacity.

"There is nothing we can talk about on this matter. You can leave now," the Ghost Scorpion coldly replied.

"Master Ghost Scorpion..."

Just as one Ear Mouse was still trying to persuade the Ghost Scorpion to change his mind, Zen interrupted them and said, "I appreciate your kindness, but I'll take care of this."

The Ear Mice who sat on the back of the giant mice looked at Zen in confusion.

According to the information they had obtained before, Thad was powerful, but he might not be strong enough to fight against the Ghost Scorpion.

"Did you hear that? This little guy doesn't want you to intervene. Mice, you'd better get out of here," the Ghost Scorpion chuckled. He seemed to become more and more interested in Zen. Zen's next words, however, suddenly made his body stiff.

"Let's continue our conversation about who ordered you to kill me. Now, tell me the truth, and I can give you a quick death," Zen said in a calm voice, as if he had already decided the fate of the Ghost Scorpion.

The women of the Fragrant Butterfly race, who watched from behind, were all stunned.

The Ear Mice beside them were also dumbfounded, and even the giant mice that they sat on stared at Zen with eyes wide open.

Only Elvinia, who stood in front of the wooden building, looked rather indifferent.

At that point, rays of light that were as thin as needles danced nimbly on her fingertips.

Recently, she had gotten more and more proficient in using the Great Sanskrit Light. The light her fingers emitted looked ethereal, and could change into almost any shape according to her will. In addition to being able to turn it into clothes, she also wanted to try if she could turn it into a pair of wings.

Chapter 3521 Dismemberment All the Other Shore creatures that lurked, peeped, and eavesdropped in the buildings on both sides of the road couldn't believe their ears.

"What did that young human say? Did I hear it wrong?"

"He was threatening Master Ghost Scorpion!"

"Oh, my God! He must be crazy!"

The Ghost Scorpion might not be the strongest Other Shore creature in the Myriad Spirits City, but he was definitely a local powerhouse. He controlled almost the entire underground world in the north of the Myriad Spirits City by himself, and even the City Guard House couldn't do anything to him.

Whoever dared to provoke him would have a miserable ending. Usually, they seldom had the chance to see the sunrise on the next day.

Yet, there was Zen, who unhesitatingly instigated such a being. The creatures on the Other Shore all thought something was wrong with him.

The Souls of Light of the Bearing race, the Sun Crow race, and other races, who stayed on the terrace of the oval-shaped building three thousand feet away, were also shocked and confused at Zen's words.

"That guy's reaction is a little unexpected..."

"Humph! He is only trying to pretend and bluff when he is dying!"

"Anyway, he knows he is going to die. Maybe he felt it was good to pretend to be a hero before he dies."

In their opinion, it was still impossible for Zen to fight against the Ghost Scorpion even if he had a corporeal body. After all, it had cost them a lot of resources to hire the Ghost Scorpion.

Meanwhile, the Ghost Scorpion went stiff for about a dozen seconds, before he finally let out a muffled wild laugh.

"Hahaha!"

As the Ghost Scorpion's laughs rang out, the female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race behind him burst into giggles as well.

"Humans are so interesting. I..."

Before the Ghost Scorpion could finish his words, Zen took a step forward.

That one step he took towards the Ghost Scorpion was over a hundred feet.

He was able to do so because he used his heels to generate power and forcefully suppress the ground, thereby leaving a crater behind. At the same time, he stretched his hand towards the Ghost Scorpion and gently passed by his body. Then, he stood behind his opponent, at the side of the female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race.

At that moment, his hand was holding the Ghost Scorpion's right arm.

"He didn't tell the truth, so I have no choice but to let him die in pain. Take it," he said flatly.

The female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race who had been cackling with the Ghost Scorpion at Zen's words, had never thought that things would change in the blink of an eye.

The wide grins on their faces froze as they stared at the arm Zen was holding in disbelief. One of them glanced at the Ghost Scorpion, only to find that his right arm was indeed detached from his shoulder.

When Zen saw that none of the female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race wanted to take the arm, he shook his head and casually threw the disconnected limb on the ground. Then, he turned around and stomped his foot once again.

"Dong!"

A muffled sound came from the soft ground once again. The high pressure caused the soil to spread out everywhere like waves, and created a bottomless hole in the ground. At the same time, Zen once again passed by the Ghost Scorpion.

This time, however, the Ghost Scorpion had time to react.

He wasn't slow to react by any means, it was just that Zen's current speed was far beyond his limit.

The moment Zen attacked him for the second time, the Ghost Scorpion chose to fight back.

He stretched out his remaining arm towards Zen and simultaneously swept his tail.

"Crack..."

Yet, Zen had gotten away from him in a flash.

Moreover, he also took the Ghost Scorpion's left arm with him! In just two confrontations, Zen had already removed both of the Ghost Scorpion's arms, but the latter didn't look bothered at all. Instead, his lips stretched into a grim smile. "Human, your speed is indeed beyond my expectations, but it's a pity for you..."

He wagged his tail as he spoke, and the hook on it glowed faintly.

He was quite proud of his tail, which could move extremely fast.

Without any warning, the tail's hook swept past Zen's waist.

Now, the Ghost Scorpion was sure that he could kill Zen with his tail.

To his surprise, however, he heard Zen say indifferently, "Have you heard of the Chaotic Source Spirit?" "The Chaotic Source Spirit?" Ghost Scorpion said dumbly.

As a master in Stage Fourteen of the Other Shore, he did not know much about the higher stages of the Desire World. He had heard that the Chaotic Source Spirit was connected with the Source World before, but he didn't think that was important. Thus, he had no idea why Zen mentioned it out of the blue.

"Your attack just now was far from enough to exhaust my Chaotic Source Spirits," Zen said with a shake of his head. "It is even less than sufficient to harm me, not to mention... I'm not afraid of the poison at all."

Zen had experienced all kinds of highly toxic poisons before. Therefore, the poisonous hook on the Ghost Scorpion's tail couldn't harm him.

Furthermore, the Ghost Scorpion's attack did not exhaust the Chaotic Source Spirits, nor did it cut through his skin.

Such were the big advantages of the Chaotic Source Realm warriors.

While the Ghost Scorpion still pondered over Zen's words, Zen's body flashed across him with two muffled sounds once again.

At that point, Zen had detached one of the Ghost Scorpion's legs.

Naturally, he lost his balance and fell down to the ground.

"Ahhh!" the female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race behind Ghost Scorpion let out a series of shrieks.

After a while, they finally came back to their senses, but they didn't seem to have any better means of expression other than screaming.

Then, two of them flapped their wings and released a gust of colorful poisonous smog. The poisonous smog could be inhaled through mouths and noses. Anyone who had absorbed it would become paralyzed and unable to move.

Upon seeing the poisonous smog, the Ear Mice immediately went away to dodge it.

As for Zen, he simply ignored the existence of such poisonous smog, and he didn't pay any attention to the female members of the Fragrant Butterfly race. He once again passed by the Ghost Scorpion.

"Crack!"

The other leg of the Ghost Scorpion was also taken away by Zen.

"Crack!"

Even his tail, which he was very proud of, was also detached from his body.

Now with only a head and a torso, he lay on the ground, unable to move.

Lying on the ground, he felt like he was dreaming.

Just now, he had been thinking about how to deal with this arrogant and unruly human. But less than half a minute later, he had almost been dismembered by Zen. He could not help but doubt the facticity of all this.

"I'll give you one more chance to tell me whose orders you're under," Zen asked.

He thought he had guessed it correctly, but still he wanted to confirm his guess.

Without even launching any powerful attack, the Ghost Scorpion had lost his arms, legs, and even his tail. It was not until then that he was finally filled with fear.

He had accepted the commission without thinking too much. Now, it turned out that he had fallen into such a deep pit, which was way beyond what he had predicted.

He felt a lot of remorse and hatred for the one who had asked him to do all this. "It's the Star Falcon race! The damn Star Falcon race!" Ghost Scorpion shouted loudly.

Zen had just arrived at the Myriad Spirits City and didn't know much about the races on the Other Shore in the Desire World, so of course, he didn't know anything about the Star Falcon race.

An Ear Mouse who was not far away explained to him, "The Star Falcon race is a major race in Stage Fourteen of the Other Shore. They occupy another city, which is called Sky Water City. They have been supporting the Sun Crow race."

The Ear Mice were well-informed, so they clearly knew about such information.

"The Sun Crow race?" Zen pursed his lips.

"Let me go..."

Just as the Ghost Scorpion was about to beg for mercy, he saw that Zen had stretched his hand towards his head. When he realized what was about to happen, his head was already decapitated.

Chapter 3522 Wealth Witnessing the death of the Ghost Scorpion, the members of the Fragrant Butterfly race took on a ghastly expression.

They had relied on the Ghost Scorpion, king of the underground world in the northern part of the Myriad Spirits City. Massive change was bound to happen due to his sudden death.

Overwhelmed with anxiety, they froze in place, unable to even consider fleeing.

The Souls of Light on the terrace of the oval-shaped building were also dumbfounded.

"The Ghost Scorpion is actually weak?"

"That man is too powerful. The Ghost Scorpion was no match for him..."

"Alas, I made a wrong judgment before. I have to go back to report this."

These Souls of Light had stayed to watch Thad and Elvinia die. They had thought that their demise was certain, so the unexpected turn of events shocked them numb.

"Buzz..."

A demon woman disappeared from the terrace and returned to the Source World.

The demon women were not staying in the Divine Lair all the time. Most of the time, they lived in golden divine trees. When the demon woman appeared in a golden divine tree, she spread out her wings and flew towards the Divine Lair.

At the sight of the flying figure, the Sun Crows rose high into the air and squawked excitedly.

Upon the arrival of the demon woman, she knelt before Elizabeth.

"The Ghost Scorpion at Stage Fourteen was easily killed by the man named Thad?" Elizabeth clarified.

"Yes, he had no power to fight back," the demon woman answered, head still bowed.

Even though she had witnessed the whole thing with her own eyes, she still couldn't believe it.

"I see." Elizabeth nodded calmly. "The Ghost Scorpion is just an unimportant pawn, anyway. Don't worry. Continue observing. Someone else will fight Thad."

The creatures at Stage Fourteen were the weakest in the entire Desire World. It didn't matter even if they failed.

However, something bugged Elizabeth.

It was very likely that Thad was actually Zen. Although Elizabeth hadn't been able to confirm it, it didn't matter. As long as she could get rid of Thad and Elvinia, she would be willing to pay the price.

Spreading out her massive wings, she closed her eyes and transferred to the Other Shore.

The Souls of Light of the Bearing race, the Sun Crow race and the other two races were not the only stunned ones.

All the creatures that secretly watched were also speechless, shocked stiff.

Everyone was afraid of the Ghost Scorpion, the leader of the underground world. Ordinary creatures didn't dare to provoke him. They would stay away from him lest they cause trouble. However, just now, he didn't even have a chance to strike back and died at the gate of the Oneness Sky Palace's stronghold.

The Oneness Sky Palace was just an ordinary force in the eyes of the creatures on the Other Shore.

The lowly Souls of Light of the Oneness Sky Palace were very careful to keep a low profile, and were usually polite to any creatures they stumbled across in the Myriad Spirits City.

In fact, many creatures had taken advantage of their meek nature and robbed them of their soul pills, and occasionally, even soul crystal.

"Is that human brat an outsider hired by the Oneness Sky Palace?"

"I have never seen that woman. But that human man has actually come to the Other Shore with his corporeal body!"

"I extorted 20, 000 soul pills from them not long ago. If they find out what I did, I might be in big trouble!"

The people from the Source World could leave the Other Shore at any time if they wanted to, but the creatures on the Other Shore couldn't. If they had offended someone they shouldn't have, they'd have no choice but to run away from the Myriad Spirits City.

Like the other creatures on the Other Shore, the several Ear Mice that were watching from the backs of giant mice were also dumbstruck, staring at the corpse of the Ghost Scorpion. They had originally planned to help Zen get out of this situation, but apparently, he didn't need their help! At the same time, they felt somewhat relieved.

At the very least, they didn't have any bad blood with Zen. Then again, if they had been able to lend Zen a hand at the time, they could've asked for something in exchange.

"Ear Mice," Zen suddenly called out, interrupting their thoughts.

With a squeak, the leader of the Ear Mice answered promptly, "Thad, what can we do for you?"

Zen glanced at the corpse of the Ghost Scorpion and asked, "Since the Ghost Scorpion has occupied the northern part of the Myriad Spirits City for many years, he should have accumulated quite a bit of wealth and resources, right?"

Hearing Zen's words, the Ear Mice suddenly shivered.

They had been so shocked by Zen's power that they forgot this.

The Ghost Scorpion occupied the underground world in the northern part of the Myriad Spirits City. Over the years, he had accumulated wealth, but with his death, what would become of it? As long as the news of the Ghost Scorpion's death was spread to the north of the city, the creatures that followed the Ghost Scorpion would definitely scramble to take as much of the wealth he had left.

"I want half of his accumulated wealth. The other half belongs to you," Zen said.

The Ear Mice exchanged glances. Their leader promptly said to an underling, "Hurry up! Go to the north of the city!"

Like the Ghost Scorpion, the Ear Mice were also active in the underground world of the Myriad Spirits City. The Ghost Scorpion was in the north, while the Ear Mice were in the south. They each minded their own business, without interfering with each other.

Now that the Ghost Scorpion was dead, naturally, this was a great opportunity for the Ear Mice. Not only could they collect the immense wealth, but they could also take over the northern territory. As for Zen's request, they wouldn't have objected even if he asked for all of the wealth! The appointed Ear Mouse left quickly.

Zen indifferently glanced at the women from the Fragrant Butterfly race not far away, who had tried to attack him with poison just now.

However, he knew they were powerless against him, especially since the Ghost Scorpion was killed. He waved his hand at them and said, "You can go now."

The women trembled slightly as Zen addressed them.

They had been standing there, not daring to run away.

To their surprise, Zen just asked them to leave like that.

They couldn't believe their ears.

Once Zen finished his words, he immediately turned around and walked straight towards Elvinia. Unexpectedly, Elvinia cracked a smirk and joked, "Those women are beautiful. Take them back!"

"What? Since when did you make jokes?" Zen raised an eyebrow amusedly.

Elvinia's cheeks flushed.

It was true that she had become quite cheerful in the past six months.

Sometimes, she'd just blurt out something without thinking first.

It suddenly dawned on the women of the Fragrant Butterfly race that Zen truly didn't have any intention to deal with them, so they heaved a sigh of relief. Fluttering their wings, they prepared to flee.

Just as they took off, they heard something whistling through the air.

Swish! Swish! Swish! All of a sudden, sharp green arrows rained from out of nowhere, piercing the women's wings and bodies.

In the blink of an eye, the several beautiful women had been shot ruthlessly by countless sharp arrows.

Chapter 3523 Black Bear Creatures from the Other Shore resembling mole crickets, stood firm and held long bows. They pulled back on their bows and released a wave of sharp arrows.

Zen heard the sound behind him and turned towards it. He frowned as he looked on.

The arrows weren't aimed at him and Elvinia, but at the women of the Fragrant Butterfly race instead, killing them all.

Once all the arrows had been released, a 10-foot tall black bear emerged from behind the mole crickets. He stood tall, strong and unmistakably domineering with aggression glowing in his green eyes.

"The people of City Guard House are here..."

"Good timing!"

"The City Guard House and the Ghost Scorpion have always been at odds. I doubt they would offer any help to the Ghost Scorpion now."

All kinds of creatures from the Other Shore chimed in their speculations.

On the round terrace, Souls of Light of the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race all smirked when they saw the black bear.

If the Ghost Scorpion was not strong enough to kill Zen, the City Guard House should be able to do the trick! "The city guard!"

"Squeak! Sir!"

Several Ear Mice bowed respectfully at the sight of the black bear.

The city guards were a special force in the Myriad Spirits City. Many races from the Other Shore lived here and were constantly engaged in conflicts with one another. Because of this, the city guards had created laws and acquired a considerable amount of strength in order to maintain the peace within the city.

The Ear Mouse race might have been quite powerful in the south of the city, but they still required the City Guard House's support and naturally had to show their respect to the black bear.

The black bear strode past the bodies of the Fragrant Butterfly women, paying no attention to the Ear Mice. He glanced at the dead Ghost Scorpion lying on the ground and cursed inwardly, 'Useless!' He then turned his glare towards Zen and asked, "Was it you who killed the Ghost Scorpion?"

"Yes, it was," replied Zen indifferently.

"Do you know what happens to those who commit murder in the Myriad Spirits City?" the black bear pressed further.

Hearing this made the Ear Mice uneasy.

One of the Ear Mice then raced up to him to explain, "Sir, it's the Ghost Scorpion that..."

"Fuck off!"

the black bear yelled at it impatiently and slapped the giant mouse away, sending it flying into the air.

Fortunately, the Ear Mouse was quick enough to jump off its back and avoid being hit.

The black bear had no intention to kill the Ear Mouse. The giant mouse could bear the power of the bear's slap. Having only a Soul of Light, the Ear Mouse, however, was too weak and would have had its soul sent to pieces.

The rudeness of the black bear turned Elvinia's face grim. Silently, she lifted the long sword inserted into the ground next to her.

Zen's face showed no emotion, but his burning anger could be felt in his aura.

"Do you know the consequence of committing the crime of murder?" the black bear asked again.

"No, I don't," Zen replied coldly.

They were enemies, so Zen had no reason whatsoever to be polite.

"By the law of the Myriad Spirits City, the killer should be arrested by the City Guard House and sentenced accordingly. Please come with me to the City Guard House," the black bear ordered.

"The law of the Myriad Spirits City..." Zen put a finger to his chin and looked at the bodies of the Fragrant Butterfly women. "You had these innocent women killed. According to the law, how should you be punished?" he asked.

It had never occurred to the black bear that Zen would fire back with that.

His face darkened and he snorted disdainfully. "The City Guard House represents the law of the Myriad Spirits City. So what if I had these women killed?" he said with his head held high.

Zen sighed softly. "What you're saying is that the strongest around represents the law of the Myriad Spirits City. Am I understanding that correctly?"

"Exactly!" the black bear replied confidently.

"Really?" Zen said with a smirk cracking through. "If that's the case, then I'll represent the law here myself!"

Before the black bear could figure out his meaning, Zen had begun rushing straight towards him.

The black bear's green eyes widened when he saw Zen's terrifying speed.

Now he understood how the Ghost Scorpion had been killed by this human! But the Ghost Scorpion was underground creature of the Other Shore. He couldn't compete with the strength of the warriors of the City Guard House! The black bear roared ferociously and stretched out a pair of sharp claws, slamming them as he attacked Zen.

Zen's only choice was to retreat in order to prevent himself from being smashed into paste.

But retreating was not in Zen's nature. He continued rushing towards the black bear, and stretched his own hand out on either side, quick as a bolt of lightning, and clutched the black bear's claws.

"What is this?" The black bear's green eyes filled with panic for the first time.

Very few creatures within Stage Fourteen of the Other Shore were a match for him in terms of strength! But the grip of the human felt like he was being held down by two huge iron doors. He just couldn't move an inch from Zen's clutches.

"Turns out that around two thousand three hundred divine megatons of force is enough to represent the law of Myriad Spirits City..." Zen's words brimmed with disappointment.

The black bear gritted his teeth and suddenly lifted both his palms. Not letting go, Zen was hoisted up as well. The black bear turned and placed Zen in front of the mole crickets and roared, "Shoot him to death!"

The mole crickets were all elite archers of the City Guard House. Their Green Kylin Bows possessed incredible penetrating power. The black bear had expected that even with Zen's super might, he would not be able to dodge the fierce arrows.

The last syllable left the black bear's mouth and he was instantly petrified by what he saw.

The archers and their bows were all broken to pieces, brown blood flowing among them.

Stood beside the piles of fragments, wiping the long sword in her hand clean, was Elvinia. She stared at Zen and said, "Let me test the strength of the law of the Myriad Spirits City."

"Sure! Catch!"

Without a beat, Zen chucked the black bear with an Other Shore Power as strong as three thousand divine megatons.

"Swish!"

The black bear flew towards Elvinia.

Zen was unable to bring the Shade Stone liquid onto the Other Shore when he was at Stage Thirteen. His physical strength was extremely limited, and the power that erupted from his body was less than a thousand divine megatons. It was enough to defeat weak creatures like warriors from the Separate Abyss race, but in the Dark Region of Stage Thirteen, such strength was far from enough.

Even the Snake Goddess herself probably wouldn't have guessed that the one who would gain the most from reaching the Chaotic Source Realm would be Zen! When Truth of Powerful Holy Body wasn't prohibited, Wild Gods could enhance their bodies with the help of the Body-strengthening Jade.

Truth of Powerful Holy Body was later banned and powerful warriors of the Source World could only rely on Chaotic Source Spirits to cultivate their bodies.

However, Zen had accidentally brought the Chaotic Source Spirits back to the Other Shore, leading to his abrupt increase in strength at Stage Fourteen.

Zen could now easily exert three thousand divine megatons of force after reaching the Chaotic Source Realm by relying on the Other Shore Power of Civilization Artifact.

If Zen had had such strength in the Dark Region of Stage Thirteen, he wouldn't have been that embarrassed, and he wouldn't have needed Elvinia's help to flee that place.

Chapter 3524 Greet Respectfully Just then, the black bear was sent into the air, feeling as if the world was spinning around him.

When he landed, he noticed that he was thrown near that delicate human girl. This excited the creature.

Sure, the human man who'd just thrown him into the air was powerful - but there was no way this measly girl could match him. The perfect prey, he thought.

What the black bear didn't know, was that the girl in his sight was Elvinia, who was frighteningly powerful even when only relying on her physical strength. If Zen hadn't relied on the Chaotic Source Spirits, he wouldn't even be a contender against Elvinia on the Other Shore.

A cold expression flashed in Elvinia's eyes. All of a sudden, she waved the sword in her hand. The hemline of her dress, which was made of light, fluttered and emphasized her gracious figure.

Her petite body burst out with immense power, and her skin appeared transparent enough to see the blueness in her veins.

"Chop!"

The treasures the Oneness Sky Palace had on Stage Fourteen were too weak, including the sword Elvinia was holding. How could it bear such a powerful strength? As Elvinia struck her sword, the blade broke into hundreds of fragments.

Just then, the moon-shaped sword radiance had managed to form. It wrapped around the fragments, and came straight towards the black bear! At first, the black bear was planning to keep the girl hostage and run away.

He had no idea that she actually had such immense power, power that proved to be a lot more intense than the man's.

At this point, the black bear was shocked and at the same time, confused about what was happening now.

How did these two humans appear in the first place? Phew! In one swift movement, the sword radiance Elvinia slashed out hit the black bear's chest with great precision, slicing him in half.

After the job had been done, she lightly tapped the ground and her body retreated instantly, making sure to avoid the black bear's body that was gushing out blood left and right.

The area around the stronghold of the Oneness Sky Palace was usually rowdy and noisy.

But at the sight of Elvinia's battle with the bear, the Other Shore creatures all grew silent, as if they had reached an agreement with each other.

On the circular terrace, the Souls of Light from the Bearing race, the Divine Farmer race, and the Sun Crow race stood motionless and speechless. They felt bitterness fill their hearts.

"That Elvinia had entered the Chaotic Source World the same time as we did..."

"How in the world did she become so powerful when she just entered Stage Fourteen! There's no way her strength in the Source World can be stronger than mine!"

"What about the other human? The man named Thad? He's very likely to actually be Zen. Do you think he's stronger than you though?"

Some of these warriors had entered the Chaotic Source World with Zen and Elvinia, while some had been staying on Stage Fourteen for a long time, like those senior members of the Land of Sword Grief. They had heard about the battle between Zen and the Evil God, making them quite knowledgeable of his existence.

They were concerned if Zen would be finally killed or not. But to some other Other Shore creatures, now that Zen had killed the black bear, it probably meant something else.

There were many Other Shore races residing in the Myriad Spirits City. But there were only three forces that could actually control the city, namely the Dark Bear race, the Giants, and the Guide Weasel race. In the past, the Giants had taken absolute control in the Myriad Spirits City, but now, the powers were divided.

In recent years, the Dark Bear race suddenly rose in power. As they grew stronger and won a fierce battle, the City Guard House fell into their hands in the end. At this point, the leader of the Dark Bear race became the governor of the City Guard House, which made him almost the ruler of the whole Myriad Spirits City.

He said that he could represent the law of the Myriad Spirits City, and this was no lie.

If killing the Ghost Scorpion could cause a commotion underground in the northern part of the city, then the death of the governor would most probably shake the entire Myriad Spirits City! Not too far away, three members of the Guide Weasel race were filled with excitement, their eyes gleaming.

The Guide Weasel race had once been a large group on Stage Fourteen, but over the past years, they had struggled to defeat the Dark Bear race.

Squeak, squeak... "Look how the Dark Bear race lost today!"

"Humph! All these years, the Dark Bear race only won because they relied on the support from the upper stages! Now they definitely got what they deserved!"

"What should we do now?"

"Well, it seems like these two humans are very powerful, but they're just passing by Stage Fourteen. Maybe we should just support them! I will report to our leader! You two stay here!"

With a whooshing sound, one of the Guide Weasels rushed out. He transformed into a streak of light and disappeared at the corner of the street.

Aside from the Guide Weasel race, the other Other Shore races also began to move.

The news of the City Guard House's defeat spread out quickly all throughout the Myriad Spirits City.

Zen took a look at the wooden building, then turned towards the Ear Mice.

"This building is too shabby to be the stronghold of the Oneness Sky Palace," he told them with much concern. "Do you have any suggestions about where we can find a better place?"

At this point, the Ear Mice were all very giddy. Since the governor of the City Guard House was dead, it put an end to the Dark Bear race's rule over the Myriad Spirits City. Hence, they would all embrace a new era from today.

"This place really isn't fit for the Oneness Sky Palace!" an Ear Mouse responded respectfully. "I might know a place that could be perfect." The Ear Mouse smiled, glad that it could help Zen.

"Well then, please lead the way," Zen said, gesturing towards the Ear Mouse with his hand.

"If you two would prefer it, you may take rides on the giant mice!" an Ear Mouse offered in delight.

A free ride was so tempting that Zen and Elvinia couldn't refuse. They leapt onto the giant mice and rode them like horses.

Though the two giant mice seemed ferocious, they were trained very well by the Ear Mice. They carried the two humans with utmost caution as they walked steadily out of the small path. Eventually, the group had walked along the widest road in the Myriad Spirits City and reached the end.

Because there were countless races in the city, no matter who was appointed the lord of the city, it would cause a quarrel among the many large races on the Other Shore. There was no pleasing everyone. Eventually, they had come up with a compromise and accepted the system of the City Guard House. And in fact, the governor of the City Guard House was the lord of the Myriad Spirits City.

The reason why the black bear was able to rule the City Guard House was because he relied mostly on his powerful strength and continuous support from upper stages on the Other Shore. Without these advantages, the Dark Bear race were nothing.

As Zen and Elvinia headed towards the City Guard House, the forces in the Myriad Spirits City could hardly sit still.

Meanwhile, the Ear Mice had completely taken over the underground cave in the northern area of the city.

This was possible only through force. The Ear Mice got rid of all the creatures that tried to resist, like the Tail Insect race and the other scorpions.

With the help of the giant mice and other mice that had very strong combat abilities in the Myriad Spirits City, they were able to successfully take over the place. Once the Ghost Scorpion died, his subordinates were just a group of weaklings.

The stench of blood and rottenness filled the entire underground world in the north of the city. At this point, the Ear Mice had plundered all the savings of the Ghost Scorpion.

When the Dark Bear race had learned that their leader was murdered, they quickly reacted. They even started to gather the strong warriors of their race to go against Zen and Elvinia. But before they could set out, they were killed by the joint attack of the Giants and the Guide Weasel race. Even the members of the Dark Bear race that guarded the City Guard House had been slaughtered.

So when Zen and Elvinia arrived at the entrance of the City Guard House riding on the giant mice, the members of the Guide Weasel race were already there, all lined up to greet them respectfully. The stench of blood still permeated the air.

Chapter 3525 The City Guard House The Myriad Spirits City was an ancient city rich in history which included several hundreds of chaotic eras.

Whereas the City Guard House's opulence wouldn't be anything worth mentioning in the Source World, it was considered to be quite a rare sight on the Other Shore. Neither the Stage Four temples nor the Stage Thirteen strongholds could hold a candle to it.

The Guide Weasel race was known for its intelligence. Once they confirmed that the former city lord was killed, they wasted no time in allying with the Giants to eradicate the Dark Bear race once and for all.

However, they didn't dare to steal any of the resources that were kept at the City Guard House upon successfully occupying it.

They focused on their main goal — controlling the Myriad Spirits City.

They knew that Zen and the Oneness Sky Palace he was representing wouldn't remain in Stage Fourteen. Therefore, there was no need for offending them.

That was why the Guide Weasel race was willing to surrender the City Guard House to Zen with utmost sincerity.

"This dress...it won't fit me."

"Nor will this one..."

"And this one..."

Elvinia complained as she picked and chose from a pile of clothing. Ever since her trip to the Dark Region, she had always robed herself with lightformed attire that couldn't exactly be considered material. She wasn't like Zen whose vague shape could be barely recognized even if he was naked.

Although she'd already become more skilled in controlling the Great Sanskrit Light and the garb she created for herself was enough to cover her decently, she always wanted to find a better solution.

There were also some women of the Fragrant Butterfly race living in the City Guard House, and they had many clothes.

The only problem was that they were too unsuitable and revealing for her taste. After taking her time going through her options, she finally gave up.

"Don't worry, Princess Elvinia! We'll ask the servants to tailor dresses for you immediately. It'll only take half a day!" a member of the Guide Weasel race offered before he hurriedly left to give orders.

As she threw the revealing clothes onto the floor, Elvinia walked out of the room and headed towards the backyard.

There, a myriad of weapons was lined up in an orderly fashion on the ground.

As Zen scanned through them, disappointment clouded his eyes.

"Theoretically," he began to speak, "some of the races residing on the Other Shore descended from those ancient civilizations of the chaos. They must have brought with them their best treasures when they fled to the Other Shore. So what on earth are these useless scraps we've found here in Stage Fourteen?"

From Zen's perspective, these were nothing but mere scraps of metal. The only ones that provided any real value were the Green Kylin Bows used by the mole crickets. Supposedly, these were specially made with carefully selected materials by the mole crickets.

Zen believed that there were many legendary weapons like the Soaring Snake Sword in the past. To his disappointment, he failed to find any of them in Stage Fourteen.

Because the Guide Weasel race was indigenous to the Other Shore, they hardly knew anything about the chaos and so they couldn't answer any of Zen's questions.

An Ear Mouse moved forward and answered on their behalf, "As far as I know, the legendary weapons were obtained only by the most powerful masters. Since they've gone on to the higher stages, it'd be impossible to keep them in Stage Fourteen."

"That's right," another Ear Mouse agreed.

Zen nodded to confirm that he heard them. He never thought getting a decent sword in Stage Fourteen would be this difficult.

As he leaned forward to pick up a thin sword to test its weight, Elvinia arrived. He grinned at her before throwing the sword towards her.

She swiftly caught and brandished it before snapping it in half with ease.

"Well," she said with a smile across her face, "I guess that sword was too fragile for me to wield!"

A look of disbelief fell on the faces of the Guide Weasels that witnessed this scene. 'Is she aware of the true extent of her power?' they thought to themselves.

"Are we ever going to find swords that are good enough for us here at Stage Fourteen?" Elvinia grumbled, sounding depressed.

A member of the Guide Weasel race hesitated for a moment before saying, "In fact, the Riverside race are very famous weapon refiners who have forged many excellent weapons. However, they all moved to the Sky Water City a few hundred years ago..."

"The Sky Water City... Isn't it the city of the Star Falcon race?" Zen muttered.

He knew the Ghost Scorpion — along with the black bear — was asking for trouble under the order of the Star Falcon race.

Both the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race were determined on killing him, their hostility evident in their revenge which knew no bounds.

However, Zen didn't feel worried at all. He suspected that it wouldn't be long before the members of the Star Falcon race themselves would arrive and bring all this chaos upon themselves.

"Forget it. My friends are still waiting in the Source World. It's time for them to return to the Other Shore," Zen informed with a grin.

The Land of Sword Grief was currently full of lower-ranked disciples who were panicking.

Things were just fine for those on the second and third floors who usually stayed in the higher stages of the Other Shore and didn't need to return to Stage Fourteen so frequently.

But it was a different story for the disciples on the first floor. Most of them just started their adventure in the Desire World. Their stronghold in Stage Fourteen served as a gathering place just like the Stage Four temples.

Unfortunately, with the new disciples' arrival at Stage Fourteen, a massive conflict between them and the Other Shore creatures came.

"It's all the newcomers' fault!"

"Why did they have to provoke the Other Shore creatures when they didn't have the power? Now I'll have to remain in Stage Fifteen. I can't go back to the stronghold now!"

"You've got better luck than me. I was right outside a Stage Fourteen temple when I left. How will I be able to return to the Myriad Spirits City? I'll certainly be arrested once I arrive at the city gate…"

"Don't blame the other new disciples. We all know that Zen and Princess Elvinia are the ones to blame. It's them you should be confronting regarding all of this — if you have the guts, that is."

Zen reached the top of the Ranking Stone on the first floor in only one day.

None of these people would have the ability to challenge him. As for Elvinia, who would dare to confront her, considering her high status? "I just want to know how those two are doing," Abdul sighed.

Previously, he had been angry with the two of them, but Zen and Elvinia were still members of the Oneness Sky Palace. Though they had physical bodies on the Other Shore, Abdul couldn't help but wonder if they were strong enough to face the creatures of the Other Shore.

Many of the new disciples stood aside and said nothing.

Soon, the deep and heavy feeling in the room became too much to bear.

Chaim finally gave in and exclaimed, "Stop worrying! Have some faith in Zen and Princess Elvinia, will you?"

"That's right. Princess Elvinia can also be considered an Other Shore creature, right? I'm sure defeating them will be no problem for her," Milo added in agreement with Chaim.

Abdul sneered and said, "Before the Truth of Powerful Holy Body was banned, taking on the physical form while roaming the Other Shore was considered common. However, hardly anyone could defeat those Other Shore creatures as soon as they reached Stage Fourteen!"

It was no easy feat to improve one's physical form on the Other Shore.

Therefore, it was never a wise decision for any new-comer in Stage Fourteen to become an enemy of the Other Shore creatures. It wasn't difficult to kill an ordinary Tail Insect, but the consequences would be unimaginably terrible once the Ghost Scorpion was involved.

Chapter 3526 Confused While the disciples of the Land of Sword Grief sulked, the door of one of the training rooms suddenly opened. Looking up, they saw Elvinia walk out with grace.

Though Elvina was someone with special status, her room in the Land of Sword Grief was still in accordance with her ranking.

"Princess Elvinia?"

"She came out!"

"Did she manage to escape?"

For the senior disciples on the first floor, Elvinia was doomed the moment she agreed to face against the Ghost Scorpion. However, she could still escape since she wasn't obstructed by the Soul Binding Thread. She could definitely run away at such a critical time.

Abdul stepped forward and respectfully cupped his hands. "Princess Elvinia, how are things going in the Myriad Spirits City?"

She gave him a cold glare. "Everything is fine. Zen just asked me to inform you all that it's safe to go back to the stronghold now."

"What?"

"We can go back?"

"How is the Ghost Scorpion?"

Elvinia retained her aloofness and refused to answer any of their questions.

The only person she was really nice to was Zen and that wasn't going to change anytime soon.

With her message delivered, Elvinia turned around and made her way back, making sure to slam the door in her wake.

"Princess Elvinia!"

"Just what on earth happened in the Myriad Spirits City?"

The disciples continued to hurl their questions at her despite her departure.

No matter how loud they shouted though, Elvinia did not answer them, preferring solitude in her training room.

Now they were even more confused.

"What should we do?" someone asked. Another disciple shrugged in noncommittal reply.

Could they really trust Elvinia's words? What if it turned out that the situation in Myriad Spirits City hadn't been dealt with? Entering the Other Shore rashly could then lead to serious consequences. It would be like courting death! Chaim, however, had already been convinced. "Since Princess Elvinia said it's been solved, then I guess we can go back now."

Milo nodded in agreement. "I believe her too!"

"Really? What if Zen was captured and tied by the Ghost Scorpion who then threatened Elvinia to lure us back to the Other Shore?" Abdul muttered in panic.

It was a bit far-fetched but nobody refuted what he said.

Everything was possible and it was their lives that were on the line here.

"I can go back first and assess the situation for you guys if you want,"

Dorothy offered.

Everyone's eyes landed on her.

"I'll go with you!" Chaim said.

"There's nothing to be afraid of," Milo told them.

Several warriors had a good relationship with Zen and trusted him unconditionally. They believed that he would never let them walk into such a dangerous trap.

Dorothy followed through with her offer, sitting down and leaning against the wall of the bronze palace. When she was about to enter the Other Shore, Abdul suddenly arrived to stop her. "Don't do it! Look, Dorothy, you're young and noble. I'm not going to let you take the risk."

He exchanged a look with Chaim who only nodded.

Both Dorothy and Elvinia had special status. If anything bad happened to them, it would mean great trouble for the Land of Sword Grief.

To Abdul, there was only one person who could enter the Other Shore and check the situation.

That look was enough to tell Chaim all that Abdul wanted to say.

"I'll go first then," Chaim said.

Like Dorothy, Chaim made himself comfortable while sitting on the ground before activating the Truth of Eternal Sword Intent.

"Buzz!"

In the blink of an eye, Chaim was once again back on the Other Shore.

He made his way into the Oneness Sky Palace's stronghold and found nothing.

There was only a little bloodstain on the outside path.

"What happened?"

Just as he was racking his brains for an answer, someone asked, "You are the disciple from the Oneness Sky Palace, aren't you?"

When Chaim turned, he found a giant mouse standing not far away from him. On the back of the giant mouse sat a Soul of Light of an Ear Mouse.

Chaim recognized the Ear Mouse's Soul of Light immediately, having seen them in the Chaotic Source World before. "Yes. Do you know what happened here?"

"Why did you come here alone? Where are the other disciples?" the Ear Mouse asked, not really answering his question.

Zen told the Ear Mouse that there were over one hundred new disciples it would have to bring to the City Guard House.

Chaim felt a bit embarrassed to tell the Ear Mouse that nobody wanted to come to the Other Shore since they were scared, so he settled for a little white lie. "They'll be here soon. Let me just go back and get them."

He left the Other Share with some urgency.

Meanwhile, Abdul and the others kept staring at Chaim's body with bated breath, scared that he would suddenly drop dead at any moment.

They all breathed a sigh of relief when he finally opened his eyes.

"Chaim!" they exclaimed once he got back. "How was the situation?"

Abdul asked.

"It's alright. There was nothing except bloodstains on the ground."

"What about Zen and Princess Elvinia?" Abdul continued.

Dorothy's eyes flickered in fear. She wholeheartedly believed in Zen but she couldn't help but be worried for him.

"I didn't see them. There was an Ear Mouse waiting at the scene though and it told me to bring everyone back to the Other Shore," Chaim replied, narrating to everyone what he saw.

His news was met with confusion. It didn't really tell them what happened in the Myriad Spirits City.

"You don't have to go in if you're afraid. The new disciples can go with me to the Other Shore. I promise everything will be fine," Chaim assured everyone before entering the Other Shore once more.

The aforementioned new disciples knew Zen and had confidence in him They readily followed Chaim to the Other Shore, believing him wholeheartedly.

Abdul could only sigh in resignation. It was a risk but it seemed they were going to have to take it. He turned to the others. "Let's go!"

Judging from his tone, it was evident that he was ready to risk everything.

The senior disciples of the Land of Sword Grief followed, sitting crosslegged in order to enter the Other Shore.

"Buzz..."

More and more Souls of Light appeared within the Oneness Sky Palace's stronghold as everyone arrived.

Abdul was the first to walk out the stronghold and saw the Ear Mouse Chaim had mentioned earlier.

The Ear Mouse let out a squeak as it regarded the new arrivals. "It seems everyone has arrived safely. Please come with me!"

Abdul's brows furrowed in confusion. "Come with you?" he repeated.

"Where?" However, the Ear Mouse wasn't going to give him a straight answer.

"You'll know when we get there."

There wasn't anything abnormal in front of the stronghold but Abdul and the senior disciples couldn't help but remain uneasy with their surroundings.

Then again, the moment Abdul decided to come back here, he had already decided to risk everything. Thus, he followed the Ear Mouse.

If something bad burst out suddenly, then Abdul was ready to get out of the Other Shore and never venture into it ever again.

The senior disciples followed Abdul's lead, walking out of the small path and heading towards the wide road.

Unbeknown to them, the shocking news of what had taken place in the Myriad Spirits City already spread like wildfire.

The matter about the Oneness Sky Palace was made known to the many races of the Other Shore.

As the human Souls of Light traversed the road, they were not met with the usual scorn or contempt. Instead, the races of the Other Shore treated them with a hint of reverence.

Chapter 3527 Sitting On The Top "Abdul, what's wrong with those Other Shore creatures? Why are they staring at us like that?" a senior disciple from the Land of Sword Grief asked in a low register, feeling uncomfortable under the gaze.

But even Abdul was baffled.

Normally, they had to be extra careful when going in and out of the Myriad Spirits City. The Other Shore creatures had always been arrogant, given their great strength. Usually, they only had contempt in their eyes upon seeing them.

But today, their eyes were completely different—it was as though there was even some kind of awe in them.

Were they suddenly afraid of the Souls of Light? Abdul and his companions had yet to realize that it wasn't the Souls of Light they were afraid of.

They would soon find out that they acted like this because Zen and Elvinia had occupied the City Guard House.

On the way there, everyone was feeling quite uneasy.

Soon, they reached the end of the road at the gate of a magnificent building.

"The City Guard House?"

Abdul was rather stunned as he stood in front of the structure.

"Has Zen provoked the members of the City Guard House? Were we brought here for them to kill?" A worried voice came from one of the senior disciples.

For a moment, Abdul was about to agree to the thought, but on second thought, he realized that it wasn't a very logical conclusion.

The Oneness Sky Palace was known to always follow the rules. They even paid their tributes to the city guards every year—it was highly unlikely for them to have provoked the people of the City Guard House. Besides, Zen was standing up against the Ghost Scorpion, who had always been at odds with the City Guard House, anyway.

'Could the City Guard House have saved Zen and Princess Elvinia?' Abdul wondered after giving it a thought.

After thinking it through, he shared the possibility with those around him.

"That must be the case! The City Guard House has always wanted to kill the Ghost Scorpion, hasn't it? But the creature has always been hiding in the underground in the north of the city. When he attacked Zen and alerted the City Guard House, they must have taken the chance to kill him!"

"Zen is so lucky!"

Unexpectedly, a warrior beside him suddenly chimed in, "But even if the City Guard House killed the Ghost Scorpion, why would they invite us here?"

Now, Abdul was stumped.

The City Guard House had real control of the Myriad Spirits City—they normally paid no mind to the Souls of Light from the Oneness Sky Palace.

What could have gotten them invited to the City Guard House? "Don't think too much. The City Guard House won't kill recklessly like the Ghost Scorpion anyway!" Unable to figure it out, Abdul ended up dropping it.

They then entered the city lord's mansion.

On either side of the mansion stood a dozen Giants, motionless like iron towers.

As the group continued moving forward, they saw the members of the Guide Weasel race standing on both sides.

All these Other Shore creatures were the elites of their races. Their very aura was strong, especially coupled with their fierce and bold appearance.

Normally, they were considered mighty warriors of the Myriad Spirits City, but at this moment, they were merely serving as guards of the City Guard House.

The grand scene before them had Abdul and the rest rather frightened, doubt growing within them. While the City Guard House had always been controlled by the Dark Bear race, they hadn't spotted any of them.

Entering the main hall, Abdul looked up at the very top of the hall. Just as he got ready to bow, his entire body froze still.

The other senior disciples of the Land of Sword Grief were also dumbfounded.

Sitting upright on the very top of the main hall was none other than Zen.

Beside him was Elvinia, wearing a bored expression. In front of her was a long, black table that had various dishes and fruits—it was a feast. She picked up a fruit and popped it in her mouth, staring at Abdul and the rest with cold eyes.

"Princess… Princess Elvinia!"

Finally, Abdul managed to call her name with great respect. It had taken a minute for him to come back to his senses.

Although Elvinia held special status, the warriors in the Land of Sword Grief were also arrogant and proud in front of her. They paid their respects to her merely because of her noble birth. But the way Abdul had just addressed her seemed genuine.

Zen, on the other hand… Although they couldn't quite see all his features, they were sure that it was Zen sitting there. They could hardly believe it! How could he take that seat? Only the governor of the City Guard House, one who controlled the Myriad Spirits City, was qualified to sit on that chair.

"Everyone, don't be so stiff," Zen said with an easy smile.

"Z-zen, what's going on?" In his confusion, Abdul managed to ask.

"Nothing," Elvinia said simply as she stuffed a dark-red fruit into her mouth. Her mouth crushed the cold, soft pulp, making a faint, fruity fragrance. The food on the Other Shore might not be much better than that in the Source World, but it sure had a unique taste. "We have killed the Ghost Scorpion, and the City Guard House has arrived to give us some trouble. I guess the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race are behind this."

"The City Guard House came with trouble?"

Abdul and the rest could feel their hearts tremble in their shock.

"But we've also killed the governor of the City Guard House, so this place now belongs to us," Elvinia added nonchalantly.

This didn't bother many of the newcomers—it was their first time in the Desire World, after all. They couldn't yet fathom how fierce the fights among the Other Shore creatures were.

But Abdul and the other senior disciples were clearly baffled by Elvinia's casual remarks.

On their way there, a strange feeling had already come over them. Now, thinking about how the Other Shore creatures looked at them in awe, they realized that those eyes were not for them, but for Zen and Elvinia.

"So this City Guard House belongs to us now?" Chaim had a smile coming on as he asked.

"Yes, this will be the new stronghold of the Oneness Sky Palace. That old wooden building was far too shabby," Zen said pleasantly. "So, you don't need to feel restrained here!"

The new disciples finally sighed in relief.

Zen could ensure their safety, anyway. It was a good thing that this place had become the Oneness Sky Palace's stronghold.

Abdul and the other senior disciples of the Land of Sword Grief, however, still felt like they were in a dream.

Just then, an Ear Mouse stepped into the main hall of the City Guard House and bowed to Zen, who remained sitting at the very top. "The savings of the Ghost Scorpion have all been recorded—there are five hundred finger-size chunks of soul crystal, five hundred and twenty Body-strengthening Jades and twenty thousand soul pills! Apart from that…"

For so many years, the Ghost Scorpion had occupied the northern part of the city—of course, he had accumulated many things. Once the Ghost Scorpion died, his subordinates took many things away from his lair when they fled, but a good portion of things was still left underground. The Ear Mice also moved quite fast—within an hour after the Ghost Scorpion died, they had already made their way into the underground of the northern part of the city, plundering all the remaining treasures.

The amount of savings reported by the Ear Mouse had everyone shocked, save for Zen, who merely waved his hand and said, "You don't have to report every detail. All these things will be shared equally between your race and our Oneness Sky Palace."

"Shared equally?!" Abdul exclaimed in shock. The Ghost Scorpion's legacy was so great that half of it was already amazing. And to think that Zen easily gave that half to the Ear Mice, Abdul couldn't help but stammer, "Zzen… since you are the one who killed the Ghost Scorpion, his legacy naturally belongs to you, as well as the Land of Sword Grief... It doesn't make sense for you to share it with the Ear Mice like this…it's beyond generous."
