After all, it had existed longer than the present round of chaos.

Both Flamine and Eastern Emperor Taiyi had travelled across the Desire World and passed by the Myriad Spirits City.

They were rather weak during that time. They faced much more powerful beings from the Other Shore and had to swallow all the insults and live in silence, just like other feeble creatures.

Therefore, they had never thought that Zen and Elvinia would've occupied the Myriad Spirits City as soon as they entered the Desire World.

"Those two youngsters are more ambitious than I was," Eastern Emperor Taiyi mused with a faint smile.

Flamine blinked a few times before she anxiously said, "The Element Spirit race is currently the dominant race on the Other Shore, while many races from the Source World such as the Bearing race and the Sun Crow race control the different stages of the Other Shore, respectively. Since Elvinia and Zen did such big acts, I'm afraid those races would take revenge on them."

"Hmph! Even if they didn't commit such acts, they still might be attacked,"

Eastern Emperor Taiyi said coldly. "I'm only afraid that the ruler of Stage Fourteenth of the Other Shore would do something against Elvinia. I'm not afraid of anything else."

Without a doubt, Elvinia's successful rise into the Desire World was great news for the Oneness Sky Palace.

After all, a purified being who could grow was terrifying.

The Bearing race and the Sun Crow race would definitely regard her as a thorn in their flesh. With her strength as a purified being, however, she had no reason to be afraid of ordinary creatures on the Other Shore, or even powerful creatures in the Dark Region. She could easily melt all of them with her Great Sanskrit Light.

Yet, there was a ruler in charge of the Dark Region in each stage, starting from Stage Fourteen of the Other Shore. It would be rather troublesome if Elvinia confronted such a ruler.

"So, I'll send a message to the two young ones and tell them to be careful,"

said Flamine with a nod.

"Alright," Eastern Emperor Taiyi agreed as his eyes glimmered with deep light. "Now, it's almost time to have a showdown. I hope that they can both grow up quickly and rise to a higher stage. In that case, maybe they can help the Oneness Sky Palace."

A smile graced Flamine's face. "They will definitely be able to help the Oneness Sky Palace. As of now, Elvinia has reached the suitable age for marriage. Your Majesty, will you arrange a marriage for her?" she said.

It could be said that Elvinia had become a purified being because of Zen.

As for Zen, he was in no way inferior to Elvinia's potential on the Other Shore.

However, Eastern Emperor Taiyi still hadn't figured out how Zen had sent his corporeal body to the Other Shore, until now.

Apparently, Eastern Emperor Taiyi had secretly observed Zen. He had faintly sensed the unique Truth of Godly Way from Zen's body, but he had never felt such an aura of the Truth of Godly Way from anybody else. Thus, he couldn't find any clue at all.

"Haven't I told you? Everybody has his or her destined mate. Now that Zen already has wives and a child, how can he satisfy Elvinia?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked back.

"I had a long talk with Elvinia after she got back from the Chaotic Source World. I'm sure she's satisfied with Zen. As her mother, of course I have to help her on the matter.

We don't need to attach so much importance to her status, but..." "But what?" asked Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

"I've heard that the old lady's granddaughter also likes Zen. I'm afraid..."

Flamine calmly explained, her lips curving into a slight frown.

Yasamin was a powerful figure who was second only to Eastern Emperor Taiyi in the Oneness Sky Palace. She, however, had a strange temper. Only a few people from the other mountains liked her. Moreover, they had a conflict last time when they were in the Vastness Mountain. That instance made Flamine dislike Yasamin even more.

"You mean Dorothy?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi questioned. There was an instance when Yasamin had mentioned some of Dorothy's secrets to Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

She had painstakingly cultivated and raised Dorothy for many years, who was considered as the apple of her eye.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi always had a headache at the thought of the stubborn Yasamin.

"I'll find a chance to sound out Yasamin's opinion," said Eastern Emperor Taiyi with a wry smile. He had never thought that his outstanding daughter would have to compete with another girl for a husband.

Meanwhile, the Land of Sword Grief had been peaceful for a few days. All the disciples struggled to contain their uncontrollable excitement.

"Our Oneness Sky Palace can finally hold our heads high on the Other Shore!"

"Occupying a large city is really something I had never dared to think of!"

"You guys on the second floor! Do you want to come down and have a look? Hahaha..."

The last comment didn't actually mean to go down from the second floor to the first floor, but rather from the higher stages of the Other Shore to Stage Fourteen.

Although many disciples on the first floor had nothing to do with occupying the Myriad Spirits City, they still felt honored.

Many of the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace scurried back from Stage Fifteen, Stage Sixteen, and even Stage Seventeen of the Other Shore. They all wanted to witness the grand occasion in the Myriad Spirits City. At the same time, Zen was so generous that he intended to distribute a part of what he had gained among the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace Previously, Zen knew that he could get more resources and support from the Oneness Sky Palace after he entered the Land of Sword Grief. And, he understood that many disciples had contributed to those resources.

Although he didn't like what Abdul had said, he still thought that he had to give something in return after he had stayed in the Oneness Sky Palace for a long time.

Once he had finished his tasks, he moved his soul to the Myriad Spirits City. Then, he went on a short-term seclusion after he had exited the Other Shore.

Even though he had shown his mighty strength in the Myriad Spirits City, he clearly knew that the Other Shore was definitely not as simple as it looked.

The creatures in the Light Region might not compare to him and Elvinia, but what about those in the Dark Region? Besides, there might be another purified being in the Dark Region in Stage Fourteen.

Therefore, the purpose of his cultivation in seclusion this time was to refine the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed he had acquired from the Snake Goddess.

In the secluded cultivation room, Zen held in his palm the seed that emitted blue light.

"If I refine the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed, will Chiyou's bloodline disappear completely?" he asked No. 9527 with a bit of hesitation. He simply wanted to obtain more blood of the Chaos Ancient God in order to become stronger, but he was still a member of the Nine Li race.

If he eliminated all traces of his original bloodline, then he would no longer have any blood connection with the Nine Li race.

"Hey, there's nothing to worry about! The Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed will not change your bloodline. It can only copy blood. When you have copied enough blood of my master, the sclerite on your chest will continue to grow. You can store the extra blood in the sclerite," No. 9527 answered.

"The sclerite..."

When Zen had merged with the Chaos Ancient God's bloodline for the first time, a sclerite started to grow on his chest. No. 9527 had previously hid inside the sclerite, and the Truth Crystal had come out from it as well.

Since then, he had never had the chance to procure any more blood of the Chaos Ancient God, so the sclerite didn't grow.

Now that it was unnecessary for him to worry about his original bloodline, he didn't hesitate anymore.

He gently tossed the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed and made it float in front of his chest. He then put his palms over his chest, which activated the Chaos Ancient God's bloodline. Green light gathered around his hands, and a Truth Crystal gradually took shape.

It wasn't difficult for him to refine the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed. The Snake Goddess had simply given him some instructions, which he had always kept in mind.

Chapter 3530 Transformation As the Truth Crystal turned solid, Zen waved his hand at it. It began to dissipate into a green eddy.

Zen gently hooked one of his fingers, then it turned into a stream of energy and dashed toward the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed.

There were six cracks on the surface of the seed, hence the name. The energy merged with the seed, slowly seeping through the cracks and flowing into the seed.

The azure blue light of the seed gradually faded, replaced by a cyan green light. The seed now contained the bloodline of the Chaos Ancient God! "The power of the bloodline is so strong." Zen's eyes showed a hint of surprise.

It was no wonder the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed was extremely precious in the Source World. Any bloodline could be directly copied by the seed once it was absorbed. It was a truly amazing ability.

"What a fascinating object!" exclaimed No. 9527.

Zen reached out his hand and pointed at the seed. At this, the seed promptly darted straight into his open mouth.

It felt strange to swallow the seed after the bloodline had fused into it. But Zen just followed what the Snake Goddess told him to do.

At first, nothing happened after Zen swallowed the seed. But soon, he felt a sharp pain in his stomach.

Zen could see that the seed had unfurled in his belly. In the middle of the seed, a green ball of light had started to glow. Each time a beam of light burst out, he felt a burst of sharp pain.

The green light was the power of Gerald's bloodline.

The power of the bloodline soon seeped into Zen's internal organs. It flowed, almost consciously, along the meridians in his body, gathering in his chest. A small sclerite began to grow out from the area.

"The second sclerite!"

As No. 9527 said this, more sclerites started to grow on Zen's chest, as more of Gerald's bloodline gathered there.

The Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed allowed one to inherit all the power of the bloodline from the previous generation, just like Zen and Yan inherited the bloodlines of Chiyou and the Snake Goddess.

Thus, Zen was inheriting the complete power of the Chaos Ancient God's bloodline! The pain in his stomach grew more intense as the power continued to flow through his internal organs and gather at his chest. The third sclerite started to grow! The sclerites emerged one by one from Zen's chest, down to his lower ribs.

Then they started to grow at his waist.

Ten sclerites.

Twenty.

Thirty.

The sclerites started to emerge from his spine, going up until they grew around his neck.

The sclerites cut through Zen's insides, causing immense pain. But he was able to tolerate it. Through the whole ordeal, Zen kept a poker face.

A flicker of fear crossed his features, however, as the sclerites started to grow in his head.

He was used to seeing strange appendages on a human body, but the head was the most vital part. An accident could cause irreversible damage. If these sclerites damaged his head, it could destroy him.

"Don't be afraid. This is just what happens when you absorb a bloodline.

Just remember even the bloodline of Chiyou could not hurt you, let alone these sclerites," No. 9527 said, encouragingly.

He was right. Zen once had three heads and six arms, and it did not cause any damage to his body. They grew quite naturally.

Realizing this, Zen stopped worrying. He calmed down and let the sclerites grow in his head! The sclerites grew in a manner so precise that although they cut through his flesh and skull, they avoided all the vital parts, therefore not causing any substantial damage. With Zen's strong ability to recover, the ruptured flesh quickly healed and wrapped around the new sclerites.

After the sclerites had emerged in Zen's head, the sclerites in his arms and legs started to grow.

An hour later, the green light of the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed finally dimmed. The sclerites also stopped growing.

"There are eight hundred and sixty-one sclerites in total,"

Zen counted, using his inner vision.

He stood up and tried to move his body, but almost instantly fell to the ground. These new sclerites still felt strange and uncomfortable.

"You'll feel better once you get used to them. These sclerites have greatly enhanced your body," No. 9527 remarked.

Zen suddenly remembered how, in the Chaotic Source World, Mount was so powerful, almost invincible. Even the Evil God, who had absorbed the power of many bloodlines, was unable to kill him. Mount had the power of the Chaos Ancient God's bloodline, and his body was strong enough to match a warrior in the Chaotic Source Realm.

He was a human being on the outside, but the structure inside his body was totally different from normal people. Now Zen was just like him! Zen walked back and forth in the cultivation room, adjusting to his new body structure. Soon enough, he began to grow accustomed to it. He started to run and jump. He adapted very quickly. It wasn't long before he was using those sclerites as if he was born with them.

"The sclerites on both sides of the stomach protect the elixir field well."

"Those on the legs bring greater support, boosting the legs' power."

"Interesting! These sclerites did not grow randomly, but in a way that perfectly enhanced my body."

Zen stopped moving with a satisfied look on his face.

"Of course! My master is perfect. Otherwise, he would not have made it from the last chaos to this one," No. 9527 pointed out, matter-of-factly.

"I want to try the truth-level theurgy."

Zen stretched his arms, and the eight hundred and sixty-one new sclerites inside his body responded accordingly.

The power of a single Truth Crystal was indeed not enough. But Zen was now able to mobilize all the sclerites in his body. His entire body was filled with the bloodline from the Chaos Ancient God. He was no longer the same as before.

"Wait!"

Before No. 9257 could stop him, Zen already activated all the sclerites. A strange scene unfolded.

Chapter 3531 The Other Shore Key All of the golden blood around Zen's body started to circulate, and the sclerites continued to unfold. His hands instantly became much thicker and stronger. The sclerites on his back broke through his skin, turning into sharp thorns.

Meanwhile, the sclerite at the end of his backbone spread out completely and extended into a strong tail.

The tail was similar to that of the Ghost Scorpion on the Other Shore. There was even a black needle embedded on its end! "What happened to me? Why did I change into this?" he complained. He awkwardly stood there like a fool as he observed the changes in his body.

On the other hand, No. 9527 and the Regal Jade Spirit were used to the change of form. After all, they knew that the physical body was just a vessel.

Zen, however, was still unable to accept it at the moment. If he had three heads and six arms, at least he maintained the human shape, but now he was like a monster.

"It's normal to change into the form of the Chaos Ancient God. Don't forget that my master, Gerald, is actually a huge scorpion. In the last round of chaos, he belonged to the Spiritual Scorpion Civilization," No. 9527 comforted him.

Zen had previously seen Gerald's initial appearance in the illusion created by the Snake Goddess, which was in the form of a huge scorpion. Still, he didn't expect himself to turn into a scorpion.

He thought for a while, and then a helpless smile graced his lips. "You are right. I will not show my strange appearance in front of others!" he declared.

He unfolded his hands again, and the green vortex began to gather between his thick palms.

Square Truth Crystals appeared between his hands and quickly accumulated in the vortex. As he placed his hands above his head, a bright green star was formed.

Despite his efforts to suppress it, it was already a thousand times more powerful than the previous Falling Star Palm. If the star fell, the training room would probably be destroyed completely. Thus, he was careful not to drop it.

The energy aura of truth level the vortex had released carried a strong penetrating power. The Land of Sword Grief's training room could block most of the energy aura, but no one expected that someone had cultivated the truth-level theurgy inside it during the time it had been designed.

Even the disciples on the first floor had sensed the energy aura. They were utterly surprised when they felt it.

"What's going on in the first room?"

"What kind of energy aura is that? Why can't the array of the training room block it?"

"It's so strange. The array of the training room was designed by a great master. But why..."

Although they were confused, they didn't dare enter the training room to check what happened. Nevertheless, they became more curious about Zen.

The energy aura lasted for only nine seconds. Zen had absorbed all the energy in the vortex into the sclerites. At the same time, all the sclerites turned over and shrank back. He reverted back to the human form in the blink of an eye, and all the blood power of the Chaos Ancient God had returned inside the sclerites.

To tell the truth, Zen could also use the Chaos Ancient God's blood power even if he didn't activate his form. But if he wanted to try his best, he did have to turn into the strange appearance, which was like a scorpion.

Now that he had a complete set of blood power, he could continue to cultivate Gerald's theurgy. The Falling Star Palm was just Gerald's basic theurgy, but the way the Truth Crystals would be utilized in the future was up to No. 9527.

Yet, at that point, Zen found that something was wrong with the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed he had swallowed.

"The Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed is supposed to disappear after being refined, but why did this happen?" he asked curiously. Naturally, he was confused.

The originally unfolded seed had fully divided into two parts inside his body. Between those two parts floated countless lines of various lengths.

At that moment, his eyebrows suddenly shot up to his forehead. "These lines are the same as those of the Other Shore Key!"

As he thought about it for a little while, the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed that he had swallowed before went up along his belly, and then he spat it out.

After he had refined the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed, the inside of the seed was completely empty. When he placed the two parts of the seed together, those lines appeared again! "Apart from copying bloodline, does the seed have any other uses?" Just then, his eyes immediately flashed.

As he recalled the Snake Goddess' reaction that day, he remembered that she had shown a rare, hesitant look when they discussed the matter of the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed.

If it could only be used to carry the blood power, the Snake Goddess shouldn't have reacted like that.

The thought of it made him even more interested in those lines! He stretched out his hand and flipped on the space ring, and a divine crystal appeared in his palm. Then, with a pinch of his hand, the divine crystal was shattered and the internal energy flowed onto the lines.

"Buzz..."

A beam of pale blue light glowed, and the divine crystal had finally activated the Other Shore Key. A map appeared, along with a Sanskrit word! "It's true that there is an Other Shore Key inside this small Six-Pattern Blood-storing Seed. It's amazing!" Zen could not help but shout.

Not only Zen but also No. 9527 couldn't understand that.

In the past few years, the Pear Hill had closely protected the Six-Pattern Blood-storing Tree so that the outsiders couldn't reach it. Only Fuxi and the Snake Goddess in the whole Source World knew the secrets contained in the seeds.

At first, the Snake Goddess didn't want to hand over the Six-Pattern Bloodstoring Seed, but over the past few years, there was no important information discovered from the seeds. Of course, it made Fuxi and the Snake Goddess disappointed. After all, the last seed was hung on the tree as their beacon of hope. They had never picked it off, and at last they gave it to Zen.

They didn't expect that there was an Other Shore Key hidden in the last seed! Zen carefully protected the seed, and then sent it into his inner world to let Geoffrey decipher it.

By now, Geoffrey was quite familiar with such things. After he had deciphered the Sanskrit word on the Other Shore Key, he said, "Stage Seventeen of the Other Shore..."

Since Zen now had the map and also knew that the temple was located on Stage Seventeen of the Other Shore, it would be easy for him to accurately confirm its position. The other words Geoffrey had said seemed to be meaningless, but they were similar to the Truth of Godly Way. With those words, he could bring the Other Shore Key straight to the Other Shore.

Fortunately, he had done something similar on Stage One of the Other Shore. "Stage Seventeen of the Other Shore?" he said as his eyes narrowed slightly.

Stage Seventeen was not far from Stage Fourteen. His current abilities could allow him to dash there in a snap.

But, why was an Other Shore Key of Stage Seventeen hidden in the SixPattern Blood-storing Seed? Who had put this key inside? What did it have to do with the Pear Hill? After Zen settled down in Stage Fourteen of the Other Shore, he decided to investigate this matter.

Chapter 3532 Invitation In Stage Twenty-nine of the Other Shore, a giant golden-winged bird soared graciously in the air, spreading out the aura of ferocity.

Such golden-winged birds named Garudas might as well be considered the number one predator of the food chain in this stage. Most creatures on the Other Shore and Souls of Light would flinch and dodge every time they came across one.

The Garuda hovered over a cliff that had a sunken path.

Though the path had existed for quite some time, no one knew how or when it was made.

At the end of the path was a Soul of Light, who had a pair of wings spread out behind the back. They resembled the wings of the demon women in the Divine Lair, except they were larger and more powerful. It was Elizabeth - head of the Divine Lair.

"Before these two had set foot into the Desire World, I had asked help from the Star Falcon race. I wanted them to use all their resources and facilities to kill them," she began explaining.

"However, we failed and the Dark Bear race was wiped out."

Previously, she had been too impatient in dealing with Zen in the Chaotic Source World, which had led to much downfall.

After that experience, she knew not to act so rashly again. She had to remain calm in order to win.

But her calmness did not mean surrendering. She had a plan, and she was going to push through with it no matter what.

However, Zen had shown a great amount of strength the moment he entered the Desire World. He was sure to pose a great threat to her race and their allies.

"Humph! We should not have relied on the Sun Crow race in the first place!" the person beside Elizabeth spewed out. This person was one of the Five-element Emissaries of the Bearing race, the Earth Emissary.

Elizabeth's face darkened at the sound of this. "How can you blame the Sun Crow race for this? The two humans are too powerful. One of them is a purified being!"

The Earth Emissary gasped, "A purified being? How did this purified being even set foot into the Desire World? You might be dreaming." There was no way the Earth Emissary was going to buy it.

When the word spread about Elvinia, they had already speculated that she was a purified being from the very beginning. She was the daughter of Eastern Emperor Taiyi, but she suddenly reappeared on the Other Shore with a clear appearance. Her being a purified being was the only reasonable explanation for this to happen.

But her presence in the Desire World had confused everyone, including Elizabeth.

It was of common knowledge that purified beings could not roam around all stages, because they were rulers of particular stages. If she had managed to enter the Desire World, that would only be possible if she wasn't a purified being. This drove everyone to wonder and debate over her true identity.

"This is not important," Elizabeth snapped. "What's important is their strength. I should ask the Star Falcon race to act soon."

The Star Falcon race resided in the Sky Water City, and proved to be the strongest race in Stage Fourteen.

"And what if the Star Falcon race fails again?" The Earth Emissary challenged Elizabeth. He did not trust anyone at this point.

"Then..." Elizabeth's eyes narrowed. "Then I am afraid no one in Stage Fourteen would be able to defeat them. All we can do is wait for them to move up to the next stages."

"Allowing them to reach higher stages would only make them stronger along the way. You and I probably wouldn't even stand a chance against them!" he shook his head in frustration. "Elizabeth, I have no choice but to report to our emperor. He will report to the Blood Assembly and have the Dark Region deal with them once and for all."

"The creatures of the Dark Region can only act in the darkness. How do you suppose we lure them into the darkness when they know for a fact, that it is dangerous there?" Elizabeth asked.

"Hey, don't worry about that," the emissary chuckled. "I have a plan."

"And your plan is...?" Elizabeth asked, doubting the emissary a little bit.

"All you have to do is ask the Star Falcon race to act as planned. If they kill the two humans, then good for us. But if they fail, you'll be the first one to know my plan." he replied with a smug look on his face.

Meanwhile, in the inner yard of the city lord's mansion, a black Bodystrengthening Jade was being held safely in Zen's hands. This particular stone could increase one's body strength in a similar way that the soul crystal could improve the Souls of Light. After entering the Other Shore, all the Wild Gods needed such jades to strengthen their bodies.

"Crack! Crack! Crack... "

With only a slight push, Zen put enough pressure on the stone for it to turn into fine black powder. He gently sent it into his elixir field.

Within seconds, the substance made its way through the elixir field to Zen's meridians. Less than a minute had passed and it was already distributed evenly across his body.

Almost instantly, Zen felt his body grow stronger a bit.

If the Other Shore Power had been destroyed or removed, all the creatures in the Source World would lose much strength. Zen was not an exception to this. His physical strength had been less than a divine megaton at one point.

Even after fusing with the Chaos Ancient God's bloodline, his strength did not improve significantly.

Though he was considered to be a big threat to everyone else, his physical strength was still very poor as compared to his Other Shore Power.

"Master Regal Jade, you said before that I would be unable to refine the Body-strengthening Jade," Zen said to the Regal Jade Spirit in his body, "but I just devoured it and everything seems fine."

Prior to entering the Desire World, Zen had never actually seen a Bodystrengthening Jade.

His first ever encounter with it was in the iron house inside the energy vertex.

At that time, the Regal Jade Spirit had predicted that Zen wouldn't be able to refine the Body-strengthening Jade, because his body was not cultivated with the Truth of Powerful Holy Body. He proved it wrong by refining the jade quite smoothly into his body.

"It's a little weird." The Regal Jade Spirit thought for a moment and continued, "I guess this means that the Truth of Godly Way of your body has a connection with the Truth of Powerful Holy Body. Otherwise, you wouldn't have been able to refine it at all."

The Regal Jade Spirit couldn't seem to understand it either, but it was probably because the Truths of Godly Ways were hard to understand. Other creatures in the chaos wouldn't understand them clearly either.

There were many features of the Truths of Godly Ways. Some of them repelled one another and some had commonalities. At the time Zen went against the Evil God, he was able to pour the Truth of Three-Energy Construction into the Imperial Sword Seal. This was because this Truth of Godly Way had something in common with the Truth of Eternal Sword Intent.

Zen felt great and happy that his strength had been improved. He didn't plan to stop after refining that first Body-strengthening Jade.

Breaking Zen's solitude, Elvinia stepped in and spread out her arms, smiling at him. "What do you think?"

She wore an ocean blue dress that had light green lace detailing at the hem.

Her dress was exquisite, beautiful, and at the same time, emitted a tiny bit of energy.

"You look extraordinary. Was it made by the Guide Weasel race?" Zen asked, appreciating the beauty in front of him.

"Yes! I didn't expect them to be so good with their hands," she said giddily.

The dress was not only powerful, but it put her in a great mood.

Zen nodded in agreement. Just then, he picked up another piece of Bodystrengthening Jade and handed it to her. "You're here just in time," he said.

"Try and see if you can refine this jade."

As a purified being, Elvinia was physically and mentally strong. However, she still had things to learn, like how to use her power wisely.

Zen didn't doubt that she could refine the jade. It seemed that the Other Shore creatures were able to do it, so it should be nothing to Elvinia.

She blinked a couple times and then took the cool-to-touch jade in her hand.

"Okay," she said and then turned around and took a seat right next to Zen.

All of a sudden, the stone in her hand shone a brilliant light. "I forgot to tell you something," she said, looking at Zen intently.

"What is it?" Zen asked.

"I invited Letitia and Margaret to live in my Phoenix Palace for a while,"

she replied, trying not to look him in the eye.

Zen was stunned upon hearing this.

Chapter 3533 An Attack Back then, Zen had first met Elvinia at the Seven Mountains Meeting.

Some time later, Zen returned home after obtaining the Shade Stone, only to find out that Lavender, Laquisha, and Nelly had been "invited" by Elvinia to the Phoenix Palace.

Furious, he had stormed the Phoenix Palace to face Elvinia right then and there.

To his surprise, the three women were actually quite content there, so Zen didn't force them to come back. However, now, Elvinia had invited Letitia and Margaret. What was she up to? "Why didn't you tell me in advance?" Zen frowned deeply.

Elvinia smiled apologetically. "I thought they were bored in the Flow Sword Sect, so I invited them to the Phoenix Palace. Besides, you were busy practicing in seclusion the other day, so I didn't get the chance to tell you."

The Phoenix Palace was not a dangerous place after all, and to a certain extent, it was actually safer than the Flow Sword Sect. Still, it was a bit suspicious that Elvinia was being courteous to Letitia and Margaret.

Zen shook his head. He couldn't figure it out.

He just said, "Forget it. Let's just refine the Body-strengthening Jade."

"Okay." Elvinia nodded meekly.

Zen thought he saw a hint of amusement in her eyes, but it quickly disappeared. She then concentrated on crushing the Body-strengthening Jade for her body to absorb it.

Just like Zen, refining the Body-strengthening Jade was easy for Elvinia.

It was more efficient to strengthen the corporeal body than to enhance the Soul of Light.

For Zen, strengthening his corporeal body meant he could use it outside the Other Shore. Elvinia, on the other hand, couldn't bring her corporeal body outside the Other Shore, so it seemed a bit wasteful to strengthen it.

However, after occupying the Myriad Spirits City, Zen had obtained a lot of resources. Even after he distributed some to the disciples of the Land of Sword Grief, there was still a lot of leftover.

Just as Zen was about to continue refining the Body-strengthening Jade, a bright yellow shadow darted into his line of sight. When his eyes adjusted to the figure approaching him, he realized it was the leader of the Guide Weasel race, Clyde.

"Sir, something is happening in the Sky Water City," Clyde reported anxiously.

Zen and Elvinia exchanged glances.

These days, the Guide Weasel race had been closely observing the movements of the Sky Water City. No matter what the news was, they would report everything to Zen.

"What is it?" Zen asked with one eyebrow raised.

"The elite members of the Star Falcon race are coming straight to the Myriad Spirits City." Clyde's small, beady eyes looked serious as he spoke.

The Star Falcon race was able to occupy the Sky Water City, and their strength was far greater than that of the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race. In the past few years, the Star Falcon race had also thought of attacking the Myriad Spirits City, but it would cause a lot of trouble, so the two races had been living a relatively peaceful time.

Unexpectedly, because of Zen and Elvinia, the Star Falcon race decided now was the time to strike. In Clyde's eyes, they were a force to be reckoned with.

However, to the Guide Weasel race, while this might have seemed like imminent doom, it was also a rare opportunity.

If Zen wiped out the elite members of the Star Falcon race, the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race would be able to counterattack and take charge of the Sky Water City.

So when Clyde saw the elite members of the Star Falcon race come out, he excitedly raced to Zen to tell him the news.

Zen handed over the Body-strengthening Jade to Elvinia, who tucked it into her space ring. Looking up to the sky, Zen asked, "How long before they arrive?"

"With the speed of the Star Falcon race, roughly two hours," Clyde replied.

"We're ready to fight at any time!"

Knowing Zen and Elvinia were incredibly powerful, the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race were confident. Banking on the two's strength, they were willing to go all out.

"Good. Ask all the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace to leave the Other Shore. You, come with me to the gate of the city." Zen stood up and walked out of the City Guard House, with Elvinia at his heels.

Standing at the gate, Zen had an overlooking view of the broad plain in the distance.

The purple light was dancing in the sky. It was constantly giving off pressure. The Souls of Light could feel the coldness if they were shrouded in the purple light, but when it struck on Zen's body, it was like a piece of hot charcoal, causing a faint burning sensation from time to time.

On the city wall, the mole crickets, carrying Green Kylin Bows in their hands, stood still. They were the aboriginals of the Myriad Spirits City, and they had always obeyed the orders of the City Guard House. After Zen took over the City Guard House, they became somewhat like his private soldiers.

In addition to the mole crickets as archers, many Giants who held massive clubs also stood on the city wall. They looked menacing, as though a swing of a club would break down half the city wall.

As for the members of the Guide Weasel race, they were hiding on both sides of the city wall. Like the Ear Mice, they were small, so they were not suitable for direct combat. However, they were agile and nimble; their secret tactic was to land fatal blows up close, which was extremely hard to guard against.

Roughly an hour later, there was a dot of light in the distance, as though a star suddenly lit up. In the blink of an eye, many more stars appeared, dotting the broad plain before them.

"What beautiful stars!" Elvinia said under her breath.

"They are not stars," said Clyde, who overheard her. "They are Star Falcons. They're almost upon us!"

The Star Falcon was a very ferocious bird, with a dazzling star-like diamond embedded on its chest.

As the Star Falcons got closer and closer, Elvinia could see their wings flapping with the wind.

"You stay here and don't leave the city wall," Zen suddenly said to Elvinia.

Elvinia didn't know how to fly. Even though she had a strong body as a purified being, it was still risky for her to face the Star Falcon race.

"Fine." Elvinia frowned slightly. She didn't like to feel useless in times of trouble.

"Thirty thousand feet!" Clyde announced.

"Twenty thousand feet!"

"Ten thousand feet!"

Clyde narrowed his beady eyes at the flying figures closing in on them.

"Eight thousand feet! Shoot!"

he commanded the archers.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! Like green rain, arrows whizzed through the air towards the Star Falcons.

From the receiving end of the arrows, the largest Star Falcon at the forefront squinted at the city wall.

It was the leader of the Star Falcon race, Hans.

Thanks to their exceptional vision, the Star Falcons could see the figures on the wall of the Myriad Spirits City clearly.

Finally, Hans' eyes landed on what he was looking for. "Strange," Hans murmured. "The two targets are in plain sight."

He didn't care about the failures of the Ghost Scorpion and the Dark Bear race.

The Star Falcon race was above all the races in the Light Region of Stage Fourteen; they were the rulers there.

The second Hans received the request from the Sun Crow race, he had agreed with no hesitation. It seemed to be a good opportunity to invade the Myriad Spirits City.

Unbothered by the volley of arrows coming straight for him, Hans simply flapped his wide wings.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! A strong wind blew from Hans' incredible wings, sending the arrows backwards till they plummeted to the ground.

Chapter 3534 Counterattack Witnessing their chief flick away the volley of arrows as though they were but toothpicks, the rest of the Star Falcon race cheered.

"The Myriad Spirits City is still weak!"

"They are too weak! This city should have been occupied by our Star Falcon race long ago!"

"You know nothing! The best way is to control it through the Dark Bear race. There is no need for us to take over this city!"

The members of the Star Falcon race cackled amongst themselves as they flew towards the city wall. The Star Falcon race thought very highly of themselves, and had always belittled the Myriad Spirits City.

So it had piqued their curiosity when their chief decided to gather all their forces just to kill two human targets.

This was unacceptable-- beneath them, really.

Due to their relationship with the Sun Crow race, the Star Falcon race had always protected the Souls of Light of the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race. And these two races also enjoyed a high status in the Sky Water City, but even so, the Star Falcon race still thought lowly of humans.

In their eyes, the humans were weak. But their human targets had even bodies on the Other Shore! "Aoo!"

All of a sudden, Hans let out a high pitched cry, commanding his troops to strike back.

Obeying their chief, all the Star Falcons spread out their wings in unison.

The diamond embedded in their chests glowed, emitting a trace of star radiance that formed a ring.

This ring grew bigger and bigger, till it was as big as their massive bodies.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! From within the ring, thousands of long and thin light swords with star radiance shot out towards the city wall. These swords were several times more powerful than the green arrows shot by the mole crickets! Squeak! "Activate the array!" Clyde ordered promptly.

In no time, several Guide Weasels hiding in the darkness activated the array that was arranged on the city wall.

The Guide Weasel race had lived in the Myriad Spirits City since time immemorial. Over the years, they had planted arrays in the city. One, in particular, was the Heavenly Harmony Array at the front of the city. This array had been gifted to them a long time ago by an ancient civilization.

"Buzz!"

A thick, white fog rose from the ground, enshrouding the whole city wall.

Once the Star Falcons' swords pierced the fog, it was as though they had landed in jelly. The long, thin swords then abruptly turned around, and shot back from whence they came.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! "The white fog is sending our starry swords back!"

"Split up!"

The Star Falcons that had been soaring in the air panicked, and anxiously spread out to dodge the swords shooting back at them. Amazingly, no one got hurt.

"Chief, what should we do?"

"The array they're using is strange... How did they bounce back our starry swords!"

However, Hans just snorted at them. Impatiently, he let out another piercing cry.

"Keep attacking!"

This order confused many Star Falcons. But since it was given by their chief, they just obeyed, and continued to form more starry rings, shooting more starry swords towards the city.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! Facing the second volley of thin swords, the Giants standing on the city wall laughed.

It was a well-known fact that the Star Falcon race was the strongest race in Stage Fourteen. However, this battle seemed to be proving that fact wrong.

How could the Star Falcon race be so foolish as to launch the same attack once more? Undoubtedly, these starry swords would be bounced back to the sky by the Heavenly Harmony Array again, no matter how powerful they were.

The instant the starry swords fell, a tearing sound suddenly came from below the city wall.

Bang! Bang! Bang! With a burst of roars coming from the bottom of the city wall, a great number of creatures in green armor drilled out from the ground. They were from the Mountain Breaking race. They had lived in the Sky Water City and followed the Star Falcon race since a long time ago.

Back when the Dark Bear race was in charge of the City Guard House, the Star Falcon race had already dug out all the secrets of the Myriad Spirits City. Of course they'd been expecting the Heaven Harmony Array! The Star Falcon race launching attacks from the sky was actually a distraction. In order to let the Mountain Breaking race sneak in from underground, they were willing to risk looking foolish.

Alas, the array's foundation was destroyed. The white fog that had been shrouding the city dissipated into thin air. Then, the starry swords shot down like heavy rain.

A Giant who had been smirking just seconds prior was suddenly impaled by a starry sword, falling to the ground with a heavy thud. Pained cries filled the air as other creatures were being shot.

"Damn it!"

Raul brandished a thick metal club. The club shadows covered Zen's and Elvinia's heads, smashing the starry swords that fell on this area into pieces.

"Sir! The Heavenly Harmony Array has been destroyed. We have to retreat!" Clyde said urgently.

The biggest advantage of the Star Falcon race was that they could fly.

On the contrary, the Giants were good at head-on combat, whereas the Guide Weasels were good at sneaky assassination. Neither of the two races had a chance against the enemy they were facing now.

Click! Click! Click! As each of the starry swords dropped, it would pierce the city wall, leaving a deep gash. In the blink of an eye, the city wall was already riddled with holes.

"If we retreat, we can't kill them," Zen said firmly, staring at the Star Falcons in the sky.

"If they want to occupy the Myriad Spirits City, they will have to land first.

Only then will we have a chance!" Clyde analyzed.

"Clyde's right. But their target is the two of you," echoed Raul, who stood nearby.

Although they were full of fighting spirit, they were keenly aware that they couldn't fight against the Star Falcon race without the Heavenly Harmony Array. It was reasonable for them to retreat first.

"There's no need to retreat," Zen said calmly.

Elvinia gently asked, "Do you want me to send you up?"

"Okay." Zen smiled.

Elvinia suddenly yanked the metal club from Raul's hands, leaving him stunned.

A mighty creature like Raul should've been able to respond quickly, since he regarded his weapon as important as his own life.

But even if Raul had been quick enough to respond, in that moment, he had felt an incredible power from Elvinia's slender arms. There was no way he could've resisted. The metal club was instantly taken away by Elvinia.

Elvinia then raised the metal club towards the sky, and Zen jumped onto it.

"Bang!"

From Elvinia's fingers erupted a powerful force, which was channeled through the club, shooting Zen thousands of feet into the air.

If Zen's body was any weaker, this strike would've destroyed his body.

Raul was absolutely dumbfounded. Even the residual force from the smash hurt his face. But Zen was able to withstand it. How strong was this man? As Zen shot into the sky, a pair of thunder wings appeared on his back.

Thanks to Elvinia's little trick, Zen flew like a flash of lightning.

Before the Star Falcons had the time to react, they heard a thunderous roar and then felt a heavy blow on their chests. Disgruntled, they lost their balance and plunged to the ground.

Crack! Crack! Crack! Zen's body had suddenly turned into a lightning arc in the air, hitting Star Falcons one after another without a break. Once his body arc hit a Star Falcon, it would plummet down, a black mark seared on the chest.

In about ten seconds, more than twenty Star Falcons had already plunged to their deaths, most of which were elites! The rest of the Star Falcons were shocked. Hans, shaking his head, tried to gather his wits.

Chapter 3535 Capture The Leader Of course, letting Zen kill them like that was out of the question.

According to their intel, there was no record of Zen being able to fly. They imagined Zen would be struck down by the human woman's club! Zen's flexible figure was reflected in Hans' eyes.

"Aoo..."

With a piercing cry from Hans, all the Star Falcons spread their wings and quickly distanced themselves from each other! This space between them made it difficult for Zen to kill them.

Zen could not fly very fast as he was relying on the Thunderstorm Godly Way to fly.

He had just been shot up into the air by Elvinia's power, and as he rose he was able to strike down more than twenty Star Falcons in an instant with his great power. But now, he began to get slower and slower.

"Crack!"

He rushed at another Star Falcon, who suddenly tilted his wings and flew to the other side, dodging Zen's attack with great agility.

On the front end of his wings were many silver spangles.

This was the magic weapon created by the Riverside race.

Garth raised his wings and charged at Zen at an astonishing speed, moving like a flying saber. In the blink of an eye, he slashed at Zen.

Seeing the dazzling spangles on his wings, Zen abruptly somersaulted in the air and nimbly dodged the attack.

But the Star Falcon race was a flying race after all, so every member could pretty much fly from birth. Naturally they were more experienced in aerial combat than human beings.

Garth seemed to have predicted Zen's movement and as he moved backwards, Garth screeched excitedly and flew in the same direction as he did. He rushed towards him rotating his body at the same time! "Swish, swish, swish..."

The other Star Falcons' eyes ignited with joy on seeing this.

"Garth's blade cyclone!"

"It will cut anything in its path to tiny pieces!"

The Star Falcons hadn't expected Zen to kill more than twenty of their companions in an instant, so their great resentment was to be expected. Of course they hoped that Garth would chop Zen into pieces and that they could then eat him after.

However, what they did not know was that battling with the physical body was the least of Zen's fears.

Garth's wings rotated crazily and rolled towards Zen, when in a flash Zen grabbed at Garth ferociously.

"How dare you lay your hands on me! Brat!" Garth sneered.

The spangles on his wings were called 'Heavenly Feather Teeth'. Each of them was carefully made by the most renowned craftsmen of the Riverside race. In order to make and gather 36 spangles, both the Riverside race and the Star Falcon race had paid a hefty price.

Except for a few defensive weapons of Stage Fourteen, nothing else could withstand the wings' slicing ability, let alone the physical human body. Even the city walls of the Myriad Spirits City were soft as mud before his wings.

Garth was startled and attempted to withdraw his right wing.

Only then did he feel Zen's iron grip as his hand didn't budge at all. Garth was stuck.

Even Hans, the leader, had believed that Garth could defeat Zen, yet he had cried for help so soon. He was considered as one of the best fighters in the Star Falcon race! Shocked at the scene before them, no Star Falcon nearby dared to rush forward! Finally, Hans flew up and swooped at Zen. No matter what, he had to save Garth first! "He is finally coming!"

Zen noticed Hans approaching as he was rolling over.

The most effective method was to kill the leader of the race first, just as he had killed the leader of the Dark Bear race and then destroyed the rest.

Once the leader was taken care of, dealing with the rest would be a piece of cake.

Hans was massive and had been issuing all the orders. Zen had long set his sights on him as his highest priority target.

"Hey..."

Zen grabbed Garth's wings and pulled him towards his chest. Garth shot at him with a shriek.

Zen curled up and suddenly stretched his legs out to bounce off of Garth! "Boom!"

Zen kicked off him releasing a power of around 2000 divine megatons.

The physical body of a bird was weaker than an ordinary creature. How could Garth bear this force? Zen's foot prints sank down into Garth's chest. The bones and viscera in his body shattered and his huge body plummeted down.

Zen darted like an arrow, at incredible speed once more, by using the counterforce.

As the chief leader of the Star Falcon race, Hans was the smartest and most powerful of them all.

He remained vigilant, his eyes focused intently as he approached Zen. He had seen how he handled Garth and this put him on guard.

To Hans' surprise, when he was still over 200 feet away, Zen had stamped on Garth and rushed to him by means of the counterforce! 'I'm his target?' An idea popped into Hans' mind.

"Illusory Transformation! Escape!"

The bird's innate alertness would probably save him, if Zen was not the one he was up against.

Hans displayed a weird movement skill. His wings rolled and formed many golden shadows which spread in all directions like thousands of Star Falcons.

"You hope to escape with just a little trick?"

Zen's gaze was fixed on Hans' real figure and he stretched out towards him.

But his hand went right through the figure like it was a cloud and it disappeared before his eyes.

This bodily movement skill was somewhat similar to the Eight Smoky Melodies that Zen had cultivated and even the feather of Wing King.

Unfortunately, using such a skill before Zen was a display of one's meager ability to an expert.

Chapter 3536 Die With Me Failing to capture Hans, Zen activated the Civilization Artifact in his body, and then a cyan feather suddenly sprouted from his body.

He felt his body become extraordinarily light. He reached out his hand again and this time, successfully grabbed Hans' tail though he moved swiftly via Illusory Transformation! "Aoo!"

Hans howled in frustration. He flapped his wings wildly, stirring up strong winds that buffeted Zen.

Now that he had been caught by Zen, how would he be able to escape? Elvinia who stood on the city wall, focused her eyes on the scene that had unfolded in midair. It was not exciting for her; she even felt a bit bored.

On the other hand, Raul and Clyde gasped in shock as their eyes widened in awe.

"Isn't that Hans, the leader of the Star Falcon race? This is incredible!"

Clyde exclaimed.

As the leader of the Guide Weasel race, Clyde had already encountered Hans in the past.

That powerful Star Falcon had shown true arrogance in front of the Guide Weasel race. Clyde was already the leader of the Guide Weasel race but he still felt inferior in front of Hans.

It was hard to believe that Hans was seized by Zen so easily, and he looked extremely miserable, "I have wanted to smash that face myself for so long!"

Raul grunted as he looked at his own metal club in Elvinia's hand.

Elvinia held it with one hand casually.

The metal club was thick and extremely heavy. It took Raul a lot of effort to carry it. However, the thin human girl had been able to hold it easily in just one hand. Seeing her toughness and strength made Raul doubt the talents of the Giants.

"If Zen really defeats Hans, that's one less problem for us," Clyde mused with a chuckle.

The Star Falcon race had taken advantage of their tremendous strength to put the Sky Water City under their control.

When their strength waned and people noticed it, a rebellion would probably take place to overthrow their power in the Sky Water City.

In the past, the Dark Bear race had used their strength to forcibly take over the City Guard House. Unexpectedly, it was not Zen who made the first move to control the City Guard House but the Guide Weasel race and the Giants. Zen's role was only to kill the strongest one, and that was all they would have required of him.

Hans tried his best to shake Zen off. He dragged Zen up and down while the other Star Falcons followed closely behind them. Fear and panic were visible in their eyes. They needed to think of a way to rescue their leader from Zen's clutches, fast.

"Kill him!" Hans ordered in a commanding voice.

The moment they heard his order, all of the Star Falcons raised their wings in response, forming starry rings.

Swish! Swish! Swish! Starry swords shot straight towards Zen from all directions, looking like sparkling golden streaks.

However, as Zen had grasped Hans by his tail, the other Star Falcons hesitated in attacking in fear of injuring their leader. As a result, they weren't able to shoot at Zen accurately.

Moreover, it seemed like Zen was protected by invisible rules after he had activated the feather of the Wing King. Even if there was a stray starry sword that luckily managed to get within striking distance from Zen, he would have easily dodged it by shaking his body slightly.

Therefore, even a synchronized attack from such a multitude of Star Falcons wasn't enough to put even the tiniest scratch on Zen.

Zen slowly made his way up Hans' body by grabbing his tail bit by bit until he eventually reached Hans' back. Suddenly, he leaped to grab Hans' neck and whispered coldly, "If you still want to live, go down!"

It was extremely easy for Zen to kill the Star Falcon right then and there, but it would produce a better reaction if he controlled him in the Myriad Spirits City! "Do you want the Star Falcon race to surrender? Over our dead bodies!"

Hans lifted his head proudly.

"You think you have a choice?" Zen asked.

Breaking the giant Star Falcon's neck was just like snapping a twig for Zen.

"Of course I have! Star Stasis!"

Hans trilled once again. In response, the gem embedded in his chest began to glow brightly, scintillating with a brilliant starry light.

"Buzz!"

A huge starry ring rapidly spread out along his wings and formed a sphere, totally engulfing his body together with Zen.

The scant space within the sphere was just enough to contain Hans' bird body and Zen's own. His large wings still extended beyond the boundaries of the sphere.

As the sphere enveloped Zen, it also exerted a resistance force. Zen suddenly felt his strength being sapped, as if he had fallen into quicksand, the resistance weighing his body down at a great extent.

Aside from losing his strength, he also felt that the flow of blood and air, as well as the transmission of sound, were extremely slowed down.

"What... Is... This... Strength..." Even Zen's speech became slurred. An expression of surprise came over his features.

"It doesn't matter what type of strength it is; I'm taking you down with me!"

Hans sneered.

A slight tilt of Hans' wings outside the sphere made both of them glide in the sky and turn towards the east of the Myriad Spirits City.

Clyde, who had been standing on the city wall, was shocked when he saw what happened. "Oh no! It looks like Hans wants to bring Zen into the Dark Region!"

"The Dark Region?" Elvinia blinked her eyes in shock, refusing to believe what she had just heard.

"Yes! East of the Myriad Spirits City, and beyond the Heavenly Dark Mountain and the Earthly Dark Mountain, there is a corner of the Dark Region. That must be where they are headed!" Clyde explained, a tinge of worry in his voice.

"Zen will be doomed," Raul said with a horrified expression.

Both Raul and Clyde were creatures from the Other Shore. They had always stayed in the Light Region as it was ingrained in them that the Dark Region was a dangerous place. All the creatures in the Light Region were taught to be cautious of the Dark Region from the moment that they were born.

"He has..."

Elvinia stopped in the middle of her sentence. She had wanted to reassure them that Zen had Darkness Fruits and candles that were enough to enable him to stay in the Dark Region, but she belatedly realized that Zen had not been carrying a space ring on his body. All of the Darkness Fruits and candles were in her possession! "Gosh! Take me to the Dark Region!"

Elvinia threw Raul's metal club forcefully. The club tumbled in the air for more than ten times then embedded into the city wall with a metallic clang.

As she launched herself into the air, she straightened her legs together tightly. Her whole body resembled an arrow that had just been shot from a bow, heading directly east! Clyde and Raul followed closely on her heels.

Raul's body was immense, and every step he took would have spanned about three hundred feet. Clyde's extreme speed was one of his advantages over other creatures. Both of them had not been able to catch up to Elvinia, but they weren't far behind her.

They could not help themselves from worrying.

If Zen met his fateful end here, it wouldn't end well for them, either! On the other hand, they wouldn't achieve anything good by going there! No one was able to prevent Hans from bringing Zen with him into the Dark Region! Although Zen had been engulfed by the Star Stasis, dying had been far from his mind. He knew that with his current body, those starry swords would be harmless to him.

But when Hans took Zen and leapt through two mountains, a dark area was revealed in front of their eyes! "The Dark Region! You want to drag me into the Dark Region?!" Zen's expression rapidly changed into a dire one.

Without the Darkness Fruits and candles, no one who had entered the Dark Region had ever survived. Zen didn't think that he was an exception.

He probably knew far more about the Dark Region than Hans, who had been a creature of the Light Region! "My starry gem has already begun to burn, and there is no chance for me to live. You should feel honored that I'm taking you to die with me!" Hans shrieked.

The starry gem was a gemstone embedded in the chest of the Star Falcons.

The Star Stasis with the greatest resistance could only be activated by burning the starry gem.

Once the starry gem was fully consumed and burnt out, it would also be the end of Hans' life.

Chapter 3537 The Light From The Crack One could compare the Dark Region to a huge, black beast that spanned the eastern region of Stage Fourteen.

The area Zen saw was part of the Dark Region's far end, closest to the Myriad Spirits City.

Hans had no intention of perishing together with Zen. He was the mighty leader of the Star Falcon race! He had a lot to live for.

However, it seemed that death was the only way to go after he discovered Zen's true power.

Swoosh! Swoosh! There was a sharp sound as the wings outside the ball flapped and carried Zen towards the Dark Region.

"Chief!" one of his followers called out. "There's no need to perish with this human man!"

"Chief, please! There must be another way!"

The other Star Falcons continued to plead as they followed behind their leader.

Only an hour had passed since their attack on the Myriad Spirits City but in that short time period, all elite members of their race had been eliminated.

Garth, so mighty and strong, also died in Zen's hands. The only solution Hans could think of in order to subdue Zen was to bring him into the Dark Region.

The Star Falcons could only grovel at his feet to persuade him not to go.

"Get out of the way!" Hans roared, his patience worn thin by his insistent followers.

He had already made his decision and there was no way he was going to change his mind.

His roar sent his followers scampering away. There was no stopping their leader anymore. All they could do was stay out of his way and let him head into the Dark Region.

Meanwhile, Zen was struggling within the ball.

The power released by the Star Stasis was strange. It was a type of sealing power that froze Zen's entire body.

He looked on as the ball took him closer to the Dark Region, his expression growing grimmer by the second.

In between the Heavenly Dark Mountain and the Earthy Dark Mountain was a low mountain ridge.

Elvinia rushed to the foot of the ridge and released her full strength, shooting forward like an arrow.

The force she exerted was enough to shake the earth.

Clyde and Raul trailing behind her could only look on in shock as cracks appeared on the ground Elvinia walked on.

Over time, Elvinia's speed decreased and she fell on a slope at the side of the mountain.

Crack! A huge crack like a spider web appeared where she stood before she was suddenly off again! Elvinia stopped for two or three times more to get a break. Pretty soon, she saw the Star Falcons and Hans rushing towards the Dark Region at breakneck speed.

A trace of horror appeared in her eyes. "No..."

There was no way she could allow Zen to be brought into the Dark Region like this! Swoosh! Swoosh! Swoosh! Clyde and Raul, who had been closely following her this whole time, were shell-shocked at what they saw.

"He's doomed." Raul muttered hopelessly.

Clyde shook his head. "The Star Stasis is said to be able to stop the flow of all energy. There's no way he'll be able to resist it."

Falling into the Dark Region had a multitude of consequences. No matter how strong Zen was, death was inescapable.

However, Clyde had a plan.

Zen's death wasn't going to be that big of a deal if Elvinia was still alive.

Her strength wasn't any weaker than Zen's, or that was what Clyde thought since she was undefeatable in Stage Fourteen.

While the two paused to think about their current situation, Elvinia began to release a soft aura.

As she did so, her pupils rolled up so that the only thing visible were the whites of her eyes.

"Princess Elvinia..." Raul called out in shock by her appearance.

Clyde was the same and could only helplessly call out for her, "Princess Elvinia?"

She seemed to have lost her consciousness but her body thrummed with power. Elvinia's hands were raised in front of her with wisps of white light emanating between her fingers.

Light wasn't something that could be easily controlled.

Most, if not all, usually scattered and formed a simple line.

However, the one Elvinia released was forming several unique shapes.

"What are those?" Raul asked.

The sight of these blazing white lights made Clyde's eyes twitch.

As the leader of the Guide Weasel race, he was privy to the legends that circulated about the Dark Region.

It was said that purified beings could create lights that had the ability to eliminate all creatures of the Dark Region.

Could it be as the legends said? Was Elvinia a purified being? There was no way! She was from a world outside the Other Shore. There was no way she could be a purified being.

However, the more Clyde thought about it, the more confused he became. If Elvinia wasn't a purified being, then what other explanation would be reasonable? The moment Elvinia crossed her hands, the light in her eyes suddenly went out, revealing her pupils once again. Her face was pale with fatigue and she promptly passed out on the ground.

Just as she fell, Raul reached out and caught her in his huge palm. "Princess Elvinia!" he cried out, trying to shake her awake. "Oh, my God..." Clyde murmured in disbelief.

"What the heck happened?" Raul asked with a helpless expression.

Darkness covered the whole Dark Region.

However, at that moment, a huge crack suddenly appeared in the sky above the edge of the Dark Region. It emitted a blazing white light that blinded anyone who dared look at it.

The Star Falcons could do nothing but watch as their leader was swallowed in the darkness and disappeared from view.

As soon as Hans entered the Dark Region, the energy within it began to erode his corporeal body.

His hair, his flesh, and even his bones cracked instantly.

Zen, who was wrapped in the Star Stasis, was able to resist.

However, as creatures of the Light Region, it was only a matter of time before they got completely devoured by the darkness.

Just when Hans thought he had achieved his goal, a crack suddenly appeared in the sky and bright light flooded the Dark Region.

This bright light completely won over the darkness and illuminated an area with a radius of a hundred miles.

"What the heck?!"

Hans exclaimed in disbelief.

They were in the Dark Region.

Where in the world did this light come from? There was no way that was possible. Hans racked his brains but couldn't figure out an explanation.

The creatures of the Dark Region were the ones that bore the brunt of this light's sudden appearance. The moment it touched them, they all burned to ashes and died.

It was in this way that the dark demon plants, which stood ten thousand feet high, and the five-color earthly dragons perished.

Chapter 3538 The Pear Hill Stronghold It was known that despite having turned into ashes, things in the Dark Region could not exist in the light.

The white light had eroded them, and as a result their ashes had completely dissipated.

Almost everything was swept away, to the point that the area within a hundred-mile radius was practically spotless and abnormally clean.

As for the creature from the Star Falcon race, Hans, he was now on the verge of death.

He had burned his starry gem, while the Dark Region had eroded his whole body.

"How... How did you make it?" he couldn't help but ask Zen when they fell down together. Apparently, he thought that Zen had created that beam of light.

Zen looked at the Star Falcon in front of him, who was at the last moments of his life. "Because we have a purified being," he said with a smile.

Back in Stage Thirteen of the Other Shore, he had witnessed how Elvinia had released such a terrifyingly powerful burst of light.

Yet at that time, the Great Sanskrit Light, which had descended from the sky, was only sustained for a short period of time. Now, the Great Sanskrit Light that came from the space crack was almost too dazzling, as if it was going to change the entire Dark Region into the Light Region.

It meant only one thing, and that was Elvinia's abilities had improved.

"A purified being?" Hans gasped.

His originally enlarged eyes glinted with anxiety.

Zen noticed it, and wondered what Hans was worried about. Before he could ask about it, Hans' eyes closed shut and he fell straight down.

Zen's eyes narrowed into slits as he looked up at the huge crack in the sky.

He suddenly felt curious. "How could the crack be filled with Great Sanskrit Light? What kind of world is inside?" he muttered.

Even Elvinia couldn't answer the question, and unfortunately it was also impossible for him to explore the crack now.

He was still in the Dark Region and didn't know how long the crack would be there. Once it closed, the Dark Region would probably be back again.

Without Hans' disturbance, the thunder wings on his back spread out once more. Zen sped up in the air and quickly left the Dark Region.

The other members of the Star Falcon race had seen Zen and Hans enter the Dark Region, but they didn't expect such a strange thing to happen. When they saw Zen fly back with the help of the thunder wings, all the Star Falcons immediately flew away in all directions.

Zen didn't plan on chasing and killing them anyway.

Now that Hans, the chief of the Star Falcon race was dead, all the other things could be easily solved.

Just as the Star Falcons had flown away, the crack in the sky slowly healed, and the incandescent light gradually disappeared into the crack. The Dark Region had engulfed the originally white-colored area, and it was once again covered in darkness.

As soon as Zen saw the endless darkness envelope the space in front of him, something popped up in his mind. The Dark Region and the Light Region belonged to two different areas, but he didn't know how the Dark Region came into being.

"Crack..."

Zen's thunder wings let out a sizzling sound. He flew up towards the Heavenly Dark Mountain and Earthly Dark Mountain at once.

When he passed through the ridge that was connected to the two mountains, he saw Clyde and Raul, as well as Elvinia who was in Raul's huge palm.

Zen frowned and immediately flew down.

The two creatures of the Other Shore, Raul and Clyde, did not react at all until now.

They just stayed there with dull expressions on their faces. "What happened to Elvinia?" Zen asked.

"Well, you can blame it on what happened just now. She used too much of her strength," Raul said and pointed up at the sky far away. "So, she fainted."

Placing his hand on Elvinia's forehead, Zen detected that her soul wasn't damaged and her breathing was even. He was relieved. Afterwards, he gently lifted her off Raul's palm and put her on his back.

"Let's go back and discuss the thing further!" As he spoke, he spread out his wings and flew towards the direction of the Myriad Spirits City.

Just like that, the battle with the Star Falcon race ended.

Zen had originally thought that things would've gone simpler. It turned out that he had underestimated the creatures on the Other Shore.

Another day had passed.

The atmosphere was busy as the strong warriors of the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race gathered together in the City Guard House.

A creature from the Other Shore stood in the front of the hall. He looked like a human being even with his blue skin, long hands and feet, and the long beard on his face that touched the ground.

"Who is this?" Zen asked upon seeing the strange creature. "He belongs to the Riverside race," Clyde answered respectfully.

There was a time when Zen heard that the Riverside race belonged in the Myriad Spirits City before.

Later on, they moved to the Sky Water City. All of them were known for being skillful craftsmen.

"The Riverside race? From the Sky Water City?" Zen asked. "Sir, all the members of the Star Falcon race have fled back to the Sky Water City after they were defeated.

Now, the Sky Water City is in a mess, and our race is also suffering. Please send people to drive the Star Falcon race out of the Sky Water City!" the man from the Riverside race pleaded.

Overall, the creatures of the Other Shore in the city had lived in peace when the Star Falcon race had controlled the Sky Water City.

Yet, the Star Falcon race suddenly became weak, so the races they had suppressed naturally started to rebel. Some races even intended to eliminate the whole Star Falcon race, as proof of their surrender to Zen, just like what the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race had done before.

On the other hand, the members of the Riverside race were born to be fond of peace and calm life, and didn't like to fight with other races. That was why the man from the Riverside race had rushed to the Myriad Spirits City, in hopes that Zen would occupy the Sky Water City right away.

"Sir, we, the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race will go to the Sky Water City. There's no need for you to go there in person!" Clyde added hastily.

Zen casually glanced at Clyde, then was able to read his mind.

The Star Falcon race had lost its core leaders after Hans and Garth died. As a result, their fighting capacity was reduced by several levels. Zen could now conquer the Sky Water City quite easily.

Unfortunately, Elvinia had been in a coma since she returned to the City Guard House. Thus, Zen wasn't in the mood to besiege the Sky Water City.

Besides, he wasn't in a hurry--but the Guide Weasel race and the Giant race were extremely anxious! Of course, he would leave Stage Fourteen sooner or later. By then, the two races would work together to control the Sky Water City and the Myriad Spirits City. That was what they had been dreaming of for so long. In the past, they could only fantasize about such a thing. Now that they already had a foundation to realize their dreams, what else could they do but pursue them? To wipe out the Star Falcon race, the Guide Weasel race had most likely instigated the Riverside race to seek help from Zen.

"In this case, you can go there and fight," Zen said faintly.

His words were like a king's decree as Clyde and Raul quickly lit up with excitement. In a snap, they were gone along with the man from the Riverside race.

It wasn't long before the news about the defeat of the Star Falcon race and Hans' death had spread throughout the Sky Water City. At that time, most of the members of the Star Falcon race tried to stabilize and comfort the other races of the Other Shore in the Sky Water City.

When dusk came, six members of the Star Falcon race quietly left the Sky Water City and flew south.

Many great races in the Source World had chosen to establish their strongholds in the Myriad Spirits City or the Sky Water City, but there were some exceptions.

For example, the stronghold of Pear Hill wasn't located in either of those cities, but at another area in Stage Fourteen. After a while of flying in the air, the six members of the Star Falcon race finally landed on top of the Pear Hill stronghold.

Chapter 3539 Evil Plot It was true that not all of the strong races established their strongholds in either the Myriad Spirits City or the Sky Water City.

In fact, many of them chose to open up a gathering place in the wilderness of the Other Shore, and founded their strongholds there. It was dangerous, but it gave them more freedom.

For instance, the Pear Hill's stronghold in Stage Fourteen was in the wilderness not far from the Dark Region.

Since the Pear Hill had settled there, some relatively weak races and even some creatures from the Other Shore had also moved to the same place.

After half a chaotic era had passed, their stronghold had grown to a certain size and formed a small town.

The six Star Falcons soared up above the town, their huge bodies covered in the darkness. Only the starry gems shone brightly on their chests.

If one didn't look carefully, the bright dots in the sky looked just like equally-distanced stars, instead of the actual Star Falcons that were flying up above.

In the town below, a white-haired ape was observing the six stars.

The ape came from the White Ape race in Stage Fourteen. The White Ape race used to live in the Sky Water City, but later on they became an enemy of the Star Falcon race due to some conflicts. At last, they were even driven out from the city.

In these years, the White Ape race had been working hard to return to the Sky Water City.

The ape, however, didn't exactly know about the chaos that had been happening in the Sky Water City over the past few days. He only knew that someone from the Star Falcon race had contacted him and asked for help. If he succeeded, then the whole White Ape race could return to the Sky Water City.

It was truly a great opportunity for the White Ape race! This ape had been staying in the small town for a long time, so he had a good relationship with the Pear Hill. Moreover, he had helped some of the Souls of Light from the Pear Hill when they had been in trouble.

When he was done gazing at the six stars in the sky, he looked at the stronghold of the Pear Hill and said, "The White Ape race has helped the Pear Hill a lot. Now, it's time for you to repay us..."

Afterwards, he walked straight into the Pear Hill's stronghold.

As the Pear Hill members were familiar with the White Ape race, none of them stopped the ape when they saw him.

The ape entered the inner area, where he found a member of the Snake Goddess race from the Pear Hill. Her name was Naomi, and she was the leader of the Snake Spirit Sect. She had been at the Chaotic Source Realm for over a hundred years.

Recently, she had returned to Stage Fourteen to guide the members of the Pear Hill who had just reached the Chaotic Source Realm.

"Whitehead, what brings you here?" Naomi asked. The ape, which they called Whitehead, sported a mysterious look.

"The Other Shore Key to the Sun Crown Temple in the north has emerged.

As far as I know, that temple hasn't been explored for two chaotic eras. It's a huge chance!" he announced.

Naomi was touched upon hearing the ape's words, and she became a little excited.

Ever since her members who had recently reached the Chaotic Source Realm got to Stage Fourteen, the Pear Hill also had been short of resources.

If she could lead her members to explore this temple in secret, then they would surely be able to resolve their burning needs. "But who has the key?"

Naomi asked.

The Other Shore Key to a temple that had been sealed off for countless years would surely be expensive if it had appeared.

Just then, Whitehead reached out his fluffy hand and thin lines appeared on his palm. "The Other Shore Key is here, but this time the White Ape race needs to earn some. Whoever from the Pear Hill wants to get to the temple has to pay one hundred thousand soul pills," he explained.

"Okay," Naomi answered without hesitation.

A hundred thousand soul pills were absolutely a good deal. She waved her tail to summon a woman, who left the Other Shore and informed the members of the Pear Hill to return to the Other Shore as soon as possible.

Whitehead secretly cackled in his mind when Naomi agreed so frankly.

He didn't care about those soul pills, and the Other Shore Key he spoke of was absolutely fake. In reality, his goal was to deceive her.

At Naomi's announcement, the members of the Pear Hill who were at the Chaotic Source Realm continuously assembled in the stronghold. The majority of them had snake tails and were from the Snake Goddess race, while the others were humans.

As the Pear Hill members continued to appear, Whitehead also kept an eye on them.

The goal of the Star Falcon race was to capture a human woman called Yan.

Thus, he needed to ensure that she was on the Other Shore.

At the sight of the dozens of human Souls of Light that were in the stronghold, Whitehead suddenly smiled and said, "I've heard that many new talents of Pear Hill have entered the Desire World this time.

Congratulations!"

Naomi felt a bit confused. The creatures on the Other Shore rarely paid attention to the matters in the Source World because they were destined to stay on the Other Shore their whole lives. Yet, Whitehead appeared to know her race well.

Despite her uncertainty, she politely replied, "Yes, they are very talented.

They are promising." "Is Yan in the stronghold now?" Whitehead abruptly asked.

Now, Naomi was even more confused. Yan had just entered Stage Fourteen not long ago. How did Whitehead know her? Still, she didn't think too much about the ape's intentions. She pointed towards the two human women nearby and said, "She's there."

As soon as Yan and Natalie heard that a temple would be opened, they quickly came to the Other Shore together. Those who had just entered the Desire World were surely eager to get a good Other Shore Token, and of course, Yan and Natalie were no exception.
