Meanwhile, Rocco joined the Land of Sword Grief long after he had entered the Chaotic Source Realm. Although his case was rare, it still existed.

"How long?" Zen didn't expect for Rocco to ask about such a thing. He lowered his head and thought for a while, then he said, "About three months."

Upon hearing his words, Rocco's face darkened. "Do you think I'm a fool? It's impossible for you to get to the middle stage of the Chaotic Source Realm in around three months!" he bellowed.

He refused to believe Zen's words at all! The new disciples around the arena began to speak and assure him that Zen was correct.

"Just only three months. Zen is one of us!"

"How could it be wrong as we all entered the Chaotic Source World together?"

"Yes. Exactly speaking, it's three months and nine days!"

At the sight of those disciples' affirmative looks, Rocco was completely confused.

Just then, Yusuf who was on the second floor said loudly, "Rocco, Zen is a disciple of our Flow Sword Sect! He is indeed one of those disciples who have just entered the Chaotic Source Realm."

Since Rocco knew Yusuf, he knew that the man wouldn't lie to him.

After Yusuf's confirmation, Rocco was even more confused. He stared curiously at Zen and asked, "Then how did you do it?"

He wasn't the only one who was dumbfounded. Some people with insight even guessed that Zen had made rapid progress ever since he had obtained the Chaotic Source Spirits. There must be some secrets he was hiding! Then again, there was actually a limit to the "rapid progress" that everyone believed. They had thought he might be only two times faster than the others.

But now, Rocco believed that Zen had stepped into the middle stage of the Chaotic Source Realm. That was not the kind of rapid progress they had thought! To put it simply, that was super rapid progress! Zen looked nonchalantly at Rocco and said, "You have also stepped into the Chaotic Source Realm. Why did you ask such a naive question?"

In order to become stronger, warriors naturally tried every means possible to improve. Moreover, it wasn't unusual that everyone had their own secrets. Why would they expose their secrets to other people anyway? As for the secret of the True Enlightenment, Zen could expose it to the Oneness Sky Palace to make contributions to the orthodox swordsmanship.

But, how could he tell the others the secrets of his body and the Truth of Godly Way? "Naive?" Rocco hissed.

"Since you don't want to tell me, then I guess I'll have to investigate it myself!"

When he was done speaking, he took a step forward.

A strange ripple appeared inside the whole arena. The ripple seemed to have come from a feather-light step, but it actually contained a great amount of power. Suddenly, Rocco had disappeared in front of Zen.

Even the disciples on the first floor below the arena couldn't see Rocco.

Only a few people on the second floor had thought of looking up, and saw Rocco's figure flying above.

On the other hand, Zen hesitated just for a second when he saw Rocco disappear. Then ripples appeared in the arena again. He was now in the center of the ripples! "He's up there!"

Zen instinctively looked up, but he quickly frowned.

"It's too late," said Yusuf as he shook his head.

"That guy can't avoid this step." The fair-skinned man echoed Yusuf's sentiments.

"Rocco is very serious this time. His step may contain 7, 000 divine megatons of the Other Shore Power. I'm afraid that Zen might end up disabled!" Ronnie agreed.

No matter how talented Zen was, his skills were still too far from Rocco's.

If he could constantly dodge and consume Rocco's strength, then he might have a slight chance of winning. However, it was almost impossible to do such a thing.

As soon as Zen realized that, he had no room to dodge. Of course, the consequences of withstanding such attacks weren't hard to imagine.

However, some of the disciples on the first floor who watched the fight felt differently about it.

Some of them looked pleased to see Zen in misfortune. But Elvinia and her companions were genuinely worried and actually cared about Zen.

It was known that Rocco was the number one warrior on the second floor.

Thus, it was too difficult for Zen to challenge him.

Despite that, Zen did not have the slightest intention of dodging this time! He slightly tilted his body, then the Civilization Artifact released majestic Other Shore Power.

He knew that even if the Regal Jade Civilization was restrained in Stage Thirteen, its Civilization Artifact could still unleash eight thousand divine megatons of force! Back when he had been previously limited by his physical body, he could only use such a powerful force while activating the Inheritance of World.

Now as he had stepped into the middle stage of the Chaotic Source Realm, his Chaotic Source Spirits were able to bear four to five thousand divine megatons of force. Furthermore, the Truth of Godly Way in his body could greatly increase the Chaotic Source Spirits' ability to contain force.

Splash! The Civilization Artifact finally unleashed the Other Shore Power contained inside it. Almost all of the Chaotic Source Spirits in Zen's body were maxed out to the limit, while the light dots of the Chaotic Source Spirits swelled up one by one and bulged on his skin.

The Chaotic Source Spirits were almost on the edge of exhaustion, but at the same time, he infused them with the Truth of Godly Way to maintain their original state.

"Eight thousand divine megatons of force!"

At that point, he directed his punch straight to Rocco's foot sole! Yet, Rocco didn't take Zen's attack seriously. The truth was, he wanted to cripple Zen, then find the secret of rapid progress from him. If he could really know this secret, he would have a chance to get a place on the third floor and perhaps even defeat Libby, an unrivaled talent and the strongest warrior on that floor.

The moment he stepped down, however, he felt a strong force come from his right foot. He could tell that the force was stronger than his own! "How is that possible?" Rocco exclaimed in utter shock. "Click! Click! Click!"

The Chaotic Source Spirits that glimmered in Rocco's body were immediately extinguished.

In the blink of an eye, the force had rapidly spread from his right leg to his whole body! "Crack! Crack! Crack!"

In the next second, the power that hadn't been offset by his Chaotic Source Spirits started to invade his whole being.

Specifically, the force that went up along his right leg travelled to his right arm and the right side of his body, then broke them with a crisp sound.

Almost without any resistance, he miserably fell out of the arena with a soft thud.

Nothing but silence filled the whole land.

Chapter 3570 The Second Imperial Edict Everyone present couldn't say anything, and they were all stunned in silence.

The disciples on the second floor just stared blankly at Zen on the arena.

At first, they simply wanted to have fun and let Rocco, the number one warrior on the second floor, teach him a lesson. Therefore, someone took the initiative to call Rocco over.

Even though Zen was extraordinarily talented, he had just reached the Chaotic Source Realm.

It was already a great miracle that he had defeated Cleon, and they believed he couldn't possibly fight Rocco back.

However, he still fought head on. He didn't rely on his strong body alone but instead, he used both his body and strength to defeat Rocco in a face-toface combat.

After he had won that round, he jumped from being the number one on the first floor to the number one on the second floor, and subsequently passed all the disciples on the second floor.

The deathly silence lasted for a long time. Finally, Yusuf who was on the second floor opened his mouth and said, "This is too crazy..." "He has directly become the number one on the second floor. My God!" Ronnie exclaimed with eyes as wide as saucers.

"I've been on the second floor for several hundred years, but I haven't even made it to the top one hundred!" another disciple commented. "What's more is that he is only in the fourteenth stage of the Other Shore Realm," the fairskinned man muttered.

Overall, the competition on the second floor was much fiercer than it was on the first floor. There were only two hundred and three people competing, but it was extremely difficult to advance even just one place.

Many people on the second floor had stayed there for countless years, and their names had remained in the same places on the Ranking Stone.

It was certainly not an easy thing for them to improve their rankings.

Chaim, who was watching under the arena, was also taken aback.

As a new comer like Zen, he naturally paid attention to Zen's strength.

Zen had unleashed more than eight thousand divine megatons of force in the Chaotic Source World, but that terrifying amount of power was way beyond what he could endure.

If one wanted to use seven or eight thousand divine megatons of force without the help of the Inheritance of World, they would have to practice in the Chaotic Source Realm for many years. However, Zen had done such a thing so easily! His growth speed was simply too fast. If he continued at that rate, he would probably leave the Land of Sword Grief soon.

Meanwhile, Rocco lay on the ground in pain. He stretched out his left hand to grab his right arm and gently twisted it. The broken bone in his arm quickly returned to its original position. After that, he continued to press on his chest, all the way to his right leg, until the bones on the right side of his body were corrected.

After that, an Other Shore Token appeared above his head. The Other Shore Token spun around and a green light covered his head, which then instantly healed all the wounds on the right side of his body.

Then he got up from the ground, took a look at Zen, and left.

It was known that Rocco was an aloof and arrogant man. Thus, it was like a big joke to him to lose to the number one warrior on the first floor.

Like the others, he was also quite confused, but it was obvious that Zen wouldn't ease his doubts. Therefore, he didn't want to stay any longer.

Once he was gone, the disciples on the first floor released their uncontrollable excitement.

"Zen won so easily!"

"Oh my God! Especially when I know Rocco is simply an invincible existence…"

"There are very few people who can make it to the third floor these years.

Rocco should be the most promising one. I didn't expect that Zen would replace him…"

The disciples on the first floor let out a sigh of relief.

Since Zen had been above all of them from the very first day, quite a number of disciples naturally felt ashamed. However, they felt a bit better when he had surpassed even the disciples on the second floor.

Now, the powerful warriors on the third floor might be able to defeat him.

His name on the Ranking Stone on the first floor quietly disappeared and at the same time, everyone's rankings went up by one place. Even Cleon, who Zen had previously defeated, was no exception.

Truth be told, Cleon had mixed feelings about returning to the first place on the first floor in such a way. Still, he now understood that he truly couldn't fight against Zen. In just two months, their skills already differed greatly from each other.

Cleon calmed down a little at this thought.

On the other hand, the Ranking Stone on the second floor showed that more than two hundred people had all dropped by one place, and Zen was ranked first. Therefore, Rocco had to give up his cultivation room on the second floor to Zen.

While all of those happened, the battle on the arena continued.

In order to compete for the rankings at the beginning of each month, the battle would last for a few days. It also went without saying that the rankings on the Ranking Stone would change as well.

As soon as Zen came down from the arena, Dorothy immediately went up to him.

"Congratulations, Zen. You've made it to the second floor so fast!" she said excitedly. "Are you going to challenge Libby and take the top ranking of the Land of Sword Grief next month?" Chaim asked with a laugh.

"Take the top ranking of the Land of Sword Grief?" Zen thought about it for a while, shook his head and smiled. "I can't do that in a month. You must be kidding," he chided.

Generally speaking, the disciples on the third floor were almost on par with the likes of Athemar. If they left the Land of Sword Grief, they would have the chance to become Oneness Governors. Still, it would be difficult for Zen to fight them straight, even if he activated the Inheritance of World.

It was simply too hard for him to do all of those in only a span of a month.

"Well, I'll give you two months!" Dorothy pursed her lips and smiled.

"Can you give me more time?" Zen asked bitterly.

"No." Dorothy shook her head, pretending to be serious. Just then, Elvinia appeared beside Zen.

She glanced coldly at Dorothy and said, "I just announced one imperial edict. In fact, my father has issued two imperial edicts."

"What's the second imperial edict about?" Zen asked in surprise.

"My father wants to see you. Now follow me to the Phoenix Palace," she told him.

'Eastern Emperor Taiyi wants to see me?' Zen thought, surprised.

His mind subconsciously thought about the Truth Enlightenment.

Fortunately, his son had deciphered the Truth Enlightenment, but he hadn't completely comprehended it.

If Eastern Emperor Taiyi urged him, he would only offer five hundred words at most.

"Why does Eastern Emperor Taiyi want to see me?" In reality, he actually wanted to hesitate.

"You'll know when you meet him."

Elvinia grabbed Zen's arm and pulled him away, leaving Dorothy stunned as she watched the two of them leave.

As for Chaim, he was in deep thought. "Is Eastern Emperor Taiyi going to grant Zen a marriage?" he asked out of the blue.

"What?" Obviously, Dorothy was shocked! When Chaim saw how Dorothy looked, he immediately realized that he had said something wrong. "It's not necessarily true. It's probably because of what happened within Stage Fourteen," he said hastily.

Although Chaim tried to explain, Dorothy was already at a loss.

Elvinia had already fallen in love with Zen, and Zen had made a name for himself. Eastern Emperor Taiyi might really grant him a marriage.

Dorothy was too reserved when it came to relationships. Now, she felt a greater sense of anxiety.

Her lips curved into a deep frown and she swam in her thoughts for a long time. After a while, it seemed that she had finally made a difficult decision.

She left the Land of Sword Grief alone and headed straight for the Origin Mountain.

Chapter 3571 Writing It Down In the very center of the Phoenix Palace was the magnificent Supreme Dragon Hall.

If there was an important guest, or any important event to be held, this was where Eastern Emperor Taiyi would be.

In front of the hall, two rows of warriors clad in golden armor stood straight, looking steadily forward, and exuding some kind of solemnity.

Standing before the hall, Zen felt the solemn aura and put a grave expression on his face.

The last time he met Eastern Emperor Taiyi was in his resting place—that couldn't be regarded as an official meeting.

But to think that he was summoned to such a great hall—what were they planning? Elvinia had also kept everything to herself.

Suddenly, a loud voice resounded from within. "Princess of Spirit Peace, Zen Luo, enter the hall!"

"Princess of Spirit Peace?" Zen blinked in confusion.

"It's my title," Elvinia merely said. "Let's go inside!"

With a nod, Zen entered the hall alongside Elvinia.

Over twenty people were standing on either side.

The golden armored warriors outside were merely Oneness Guards, but the people inside were different—almost every one of them emitted an outstandingly strong aura. Zen even spotted Athemar and Goran standing among them.

"These people..."

Zen observed his periphery and was rather shocked at what he found.

The people were arranged from front to back according to their strength levels.

As Oneness Governors, both Athemar and Goran could only be ranked at about the tenth place. The two in the back emitted a deep, unpredictable aura, not much weaker than that of Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

These were probably the pillars of the Oneness Mountain or even the Oneness Sky Palace.

Quietly, Zen observed them from the corner of his eyes—they were staring at Zen with a burning gaze.

All of them had heard of Zen, but apart from Athemar and some others, it was the first time they had met him in person. Legends of Zen on the Other Shore piqued their curiosity.

After walking along the hall, Zen bowed before Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

The latter smiled and asked, "Zen, you've been in the Land of Sword Grief for almost two months. You must have made rapid progress. I heard that you are ranked first on the first floor now?"

Hearing the emperor's words had all the strong warriors on both sides of the hall widen their eyes in shock.

Only two months after entering the Land of Sword Grief, Zen was already ranked first on the first floor.

Such rapid improvement was unheard of.

Zen was clearly no ordinary talent.

"Father, Zen has ranked first on the first day he entered the Land of Sword Grief. Today, he has already defeated Rocco and now ranks first on the second floor," Elvinia said indifferently, as though the news wasn't insanely shocking.

The news of Zen defeating Rocco hadn't yet spread within the Oneness Sky Palace. Surely, Eastern Emperor Taiyi and his high-ranking officials hadn't heard of it.

"You defeated Rocco?" An old man next to Athemar looked at Zen in disbelief.

The latter merely nodded.

Smiling, Athemar said, "I heard your nephew was trying to break through to the third floor… but Zen defeated him. How unexpected."

The old man smiled bitterly and shook his head. "My nephew is arrogant, but he was defeated by someone who entered the Chaotic Source Realm just a little over three months ago. I'm afraid it will be difficult for him to accept the fact."

The fact that Zen ranked first on the first floor within two months was already highly shocking to these high-ranking officials.

But to think that Zen had become first on the second floor as well...his progress was amazing.

It was simply unheard of in the Land of Sword Grief. Even if Zen had obtained another powerful Other Shore Token, he still had to follow the rules of the Land of Sword Grief.

In the Land of Sword Grief, people were forbidden to use the abilities of Other Shore Tokens. Instead, they could only use the Other Shore Power to fight against each other. Because the Land of Sword Grief merely tested their Other Shore Power and Chaotic Source Spirits, no special tricks were allowed on the battleground.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi was stunned upon hearing Elvinia's words. "Zen, are you really ranked first on the second floor?" he asked Zen.

"It's absolutely true. If you don't believe it, you can go check the Ranking Stone yourself," Elvinia continued.

She wasn't surprised that he was still in disbelief, not having seen the rankings with his own eyes.

But Elvinia's look was so serious that no one present believed she could be lying.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi nodded and said, "I do believe it. But it's just too incredible."

Gracefully, he shifted the subject. "Zen, you've been in the Land of Sword Grief for some time. Have you deciphered more of the Truth Enlightenment?"

At the mention of the Truth Enlightenment, all the high-ranking officials had their ears perk up.

The Truth Enlightenment that Zen had handed over was first passed down among the hands of these people. While there were only two hundred words, they had benefited a great deal, drastically increasing their strength.

If they could cultivate the complete Truth Enlightenment, they'd definitely undergo qualitative changes.

'As expected...' Zen murmured inwardly.

That confirmed that Eastern Emperor Taiyi was indeed targeting the Truth Enlightenment.

Since he had planned to expose the Truth Enlightenment to the public, it wasn't really difficult for him to tell them about it.

But Zen still felt that something was wrong—if Eastern Emperor Taiyi only wanted the Truth Enlightenment, there was no need for him to summon so many of them.

"Yes," Zen said, ignoring his lingering confusion. "I've deciphered the Truth Enlightenment to five hundred words. Shall I hand it to you later or write it down here?"

The high-ranking officials there could obtain the Truth Enlightenment no matter how Zen offered it. The difference lay in whether it was handed over to them by Zen or by Eastern Emperor Taiyi himself.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi invitingly gestured at Zen and said, "These old officials are all old friends of mine. There's no need to hide anything from them, Zen. You can write it down here and they can observe as they like."

"Okay."

Nodding in agreement, Zen gently pressed the space ring on his finger. A single sheet of paper appeared in the air, along with a brush, which he promptly grabbed.

Swoosh! Swoosh! Swoosh! "For warriors and soldiers, they build their bodies with clarity of mind and comprehension of the heart…"

Zen's words vigorously appeared on the sheet of paper.

Meanwhile, the high-ranking officials stared hard at the sheet, afraid of missing a single detail.

But after a while of staring, they all felt dizziness come over them. A middle-aged man of lower strength even fainted.

That had Zen pause for a moment. "Masters, comprehending this Truth Enlightenment cannot be accomplished overnight. If you cultivate it forcefully, I'm afraid it will hurt your souls."

Cultivating the Truth Enlightenment was much more difficult than cultivating the Truth of Eternal Sword Intent. Even for both Zen and Eastern Emperor Taiyi, it was difficult to speed up their cultivation. In fact, it was also difficult for them to read it.

The high-ranking officials were all well aware of this, even more so than Zen, but they didn't want to waste a single moment of this opportunity. As they tried to comprehend it rapidly, their Souls of Light naturally took some damage.

Fortunately, all the high-ranking officials were powerful people. After a few seconds, the man who had just fainted woke right back up. He got up from the ground on his own, bowed before Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and retreated to the side.

Chapter 3572 A Gracious Reward It wasn't long before five hundred words were already put on the paper.

Zen gently placed the brush down and stored it in his space ring. He turned to Eastern Emperor Taiyi. "I have written down all that I have deciphered, Your Majesty."

Eastern Emperor Taiyi beamed happily as he gazed at the output.

He still hadn't figured out how Zen could decipher Sanskrit words. He thought it was blind guessing, at first. However, Eastern Emperor Taiyi himself was proficient in deciphering Sanskrit words, and he knew one couldn't get this far just by guessing.

He had no doubt that with Zen's help, they would soon decipher the full text of the Truth Enlightenment. Eastern Emperor Taiyi was thrilled at the thought.

"If we can decipher the Truth Enlightenment completely, it will be a great boon to the Oneness Sky Palace," Eastern Emperor Taiyi said, a bright smile on his face.

The Oneness Governors and other high-ranking officials nodded their heads in agreement, proud and excited of this development. None more so than Athemar.

He thought of how fortunate they were that Zen had joined the Sword Light Palace. Athemar had never imagined he would make such great contributions to the Oneness Sky Palace.

Given Zen's talent, he would probably prove even more valuable in the future. Athemar looked forward to seeing him accomplish more as time went by.

"It is my honor, Your Majesty," Zen responded, modestly.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi turned his smile on Zen. "But there is another reason why I called you here today."

At these words, Elvinia, who had been standing beside Zen, stared at the ground and began to blush shyly, a rare sight to see.

"How else may I help you, Your Majesty?" Zen asked, confused.

He had noticed that this occasion seemed unusually grand, but the thought had left his mind as he concentrated on his earlier task.

At this moment, a pleasant voice rang out, "Do you remember that I promised I would reward you graciously?"

Flamine walked out from the back of the palace.

She was dressed in fiery red silk, with fire phoenixes hanging at her cuffs and waist. She looked utterly regal and glamorous.

"Reward me graciously?"

Zen had to rack his brains before realizing what Flamine was talking about.

He had forgotten all about it until she mentioned it again just now.

Back then, Zen and Elvinia were trapped in the Dark Region, facing mortal danger. Only after they were stuck in the light column were they able to leave the Other Shore and come back to the Source World. Even so, they were still in danger then.

Flamine had asked Zen then to protect her daughter, promising to reward him for her safe return.

In fact, Zen hadn't paid much attention to those words. By the time they left the Dark Region, Elvinia had already become a purified being, while Zen had obtained the Civilization Artifact, which was all the reward he wanted.

There was also the matter of Elvinia coming back with her Memory Flame in disarray, her intelligence temporarily degenerating to that of a child's.

Flamine had been very upset about that and forgot the reward thing.

That she would now bring up it, however, came as a surprise.

"I do remember you saying something of the sort, Lady Flamine, but what reward will you give me?" Zen asked, carefully.

Flamine chuckled and looked at Elvinia. "The gracious reward is right by your side," she pronounced.

Zen turned his startled eyes on Elvinia. Seeing her blush and fidget made him realize what was happening. "Lady Flamine, do you mean...?"

"I want Elvinia to marry you," Flamine declared flatly.

Hearing this, Zen's heart dropped.

This was starting to look like a complicated mess.

"Would you take my daughter's hand in marriage?" Eastern Emperor Taiyi asked seriously.

The high-ranking officials flanking both sides of the hall turned to look at Zen expectantly.

They thought it would be a perfect match.

Although Zen was cultivating in the Oneness Sky Palace, he still joined them as an outsider, since he had the bloodline of the Nine Li race If he married Elvinia, he would truly be part of the Oneness Sky Palace.

Zen straightened up, cupping one hand over the other in front of him respectfully. "Your Majesty, Lady Flamine, I already have a principal wife."

Elvinia was the daughter of Eastern Emperor Taiyi. She couldn't compromise her status by being a concubine of Zen, could she? But Zen had been together with Letitia for so long. Surely, he would never forgive himself if he suddenly gave her up for another.

"Of course I know that," Flamine responded gracefully. "But once Elvinia marries you, she will have that status. She is, after all, my beloved daughter with Eastern Emperor Taiyi, and can settle for nothing less. Even your principal wife understands this, and has given her consent."

Zen's eyebrows shot up at these words. "Tia has agreed to this, Lady Flamine? She said this personally?"

Zen had been so busy on the Other Shore of late that he had had no time to visit Letitia and the others at the Flow Sword Sect. He remembered, however, Elvinia telling him that Letitia would be taken to the Phoenix Palace.

Zen thought it was unusual, at the time, but he didn't worry too much about it. He knew Letitia would be safe in the Phoenix Palace, at least.

It dawned on Zen now why Letitia and Margaret had been brought here.

"Of course. It came directly from her," Flamine said, nodding emphatically.

Zen glanced at Elvinia before speaking again. "May I see Tia, then?"

Zen indeed had plans to visit Letitia and the others now that he had also been summoned here to the Phoenix Palace. But the developments of this visit so far had been completely unexpected.

Flamine blinked slightly before regaining her composure. "They are cultivating in seclusion in the Heavenly Cultivation Palace. They have activated the Soul Fire Swirl. I'm afraid it's not appropriate to interrupt them at this moment."

The Soul Fire Swirl was a kind of cultivation method in the Heavenly Cultivation Palace. Flamine wouldn't lie to Zen, would she? On the other hand, Zen thought, she could very easily manipulate others into thinking what she wanted.

Elvinia almost looked pitiful by Zen's side, her wide eyes gazing at him hopefully.

She desperately wished he wouldn't let her down now. Today, her father had summoned all the high-ranking officials to the palace, supposedly for the deciphering of the Truth Enlightenment. However, his real purpose was to seal the marriage, in front of witnesses.

"You are overthinking this, Zen. This is a wonderful thing," Athemar told him, gently.

"That's right! You seem to love each other. What else is there to consider?"

another high-ranking official chimed in.

Zen barely glanced at them before responding to Flamine, "My apologies. I just cannot decide without consulting Letitia myself. Please excuse my leave."

He turned around and walked out.

The high-ranking officials in the Phoenix Palace grew abuzz, turning to each other in astonishment and confusion.

The old man beside Eastern Emperor Taiyi, in particular, was seething. He had gone to countless life-and-death battles with Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

The two of them were like brothers.

It angered him to see Zen daring to humiliate Eastern Emperor Taiyi like this.

"Stop, you brat!" the old man roared furiously.

A terrifying aura rushed from inside the hall, seemingly chasing after Zen.

The guards in golden armor posted outside the hall trembled.

Zen continued to stride out purposefully even as this threat hounded him.

Chapter 3573 I Also Want To Know The Answer Seeing Zen so unaffected, the old man's rage only flared up further.

With a hot temper, he would never let Zen get away easily! ROAR! The old man moved to grab Zen, his clawed hand launching a huge blue wolf head straight at him.

But just as the snarling phantom was about to snap at its target, Eastern Emperor Taiyi raised his hand, making it disappear in thin air.

The old man turned to look at Eastern Emperor Taiyi, surprised at the interruption.

Eastern Emperor Taiyi shook his head. "Pearce, calm down. Zen is stubborn. It would do no good to force him to stay."

"Humph! He was offered a rare chance only so few are blessed with over generations! Yet, he showed no gratitude and even walked out arrogantly! How can I just stand for it?" Pearce ranted angrily.

A hint of helplessness dimmed Flamine's beautiful eyes. "It's all my fault. I just arranged everything without considering Zen's feelings," she said guiltily.

Naturally, Flamine deemed her daughter the best girl in the world. It never occurred to her any man would refuse her.

Flamine never expected Zen would react so defensively to keep his principal wife.

Flamine turned to look at Elvinia apologetically. She felt sorry for her daughter the most.

Elvinia had changed so much around Zen, her character growing for the better. It had made Flamine so happy.

Elvinia must feel devastated right about now.

But to Flamine's surprise, Elvinia's expression remained neutral. Elvinia returned her mother's stare. "He's probably headed for the Heavenly Cultivation Palace. I'll go and have a look."

With these words, Elvinia strode out the Supreme Dragon Hall and headed for the Heavenly Cultivation Palace.

In the Fire Bearing Hall of the Heavenly Cultivation Palace, Letitia, Margaret, Lavender, Nelly, and Laquisha sat cross-legged on the floor. A burning red chain hung above their heads, emitting waves of scorching heat.

This was the Soul Fire Swirl, a unique cultivation method in the Heavenly Cultivation Palace.

Lavender, Nelly and Laquisha had made great progress with their cultivation.

Letitia and Margaret, meanwhile, had been here for only a month, so they had some ways to go.

However, Letitia cherished this opportunity very much. She knew she would never catch up with Zen, but she didn't want to lag too far behind in terms of cultivation. She took all her training thus far very seriously.

In contrast, Margaret was purposefully proceeding slowly.

As she sat, she moved her hands over her abdomen. Streaks of purple light gathered around her belly, which had started to swell.

Over the years, only Letitia, among all Zen's women, had borne him a child.

This had made Margaret anxious, but she couldn't do anything about it.

Last time Zen had returned from the Chaotic Source World, he had stayed in the independent courtyard house for days. About two months after Zen left for the Land of Sword Grief, Margaret had discovered the good news within her.

Because it hadn't been that long, the change in her body wasn't noticeable yet. Margaret decided to keep it a secret for now.

Just as Margaret touched her belly, Zen stepped into the Fire Bearing Hall.

When he saw that Letitia and his other partners were safe and sound, he was slightly relieved. Although he didn't think Flamine would do anything to harm them, he had still gotten worried when she mentioned Letitia.

When Zen's eyes fell on Margaret, she was lost in thought and hadn't noticed his arrival. But he immediately sensed the change in her. He walked quickly up to her, his face shining with joy. "Margaret, are you...?"

Margaret hadn't been expecting Zen. But now seeing Zen apparently wise to her pregnancy, a shy smile blossomed on her lips. "After I came to the Phoenix Palace, I couldn't leave as I wished, so I didn't know how to tell you. I'm sorry," she whispered.

Upon discovering she was pregnant, Margaret had wanted to inform Zen immediately.

However, as she was new to the Phoenix Palace and had no servants to order to relay the message, she could only wait for Zen's return and protect the growing baby in her womb.

Zen's sudden presence here was a pleasant surprise.

Although Margaret lowered her voice, Letitia still overheard everything.

"You should have told me you are pregnant! You shouldn't have subjected yourself to the Soul Fire Swirl in your condition," Letitia said reproachfully.

Margaret scoffed at that. "Why would I tell you first?"

Although she and Letitia had been on good terms for a long time now, she wanted to share the news with Zen first. It would have been awkward to tell Letitia, of all people.

"But Margaret, it is dangerous to cultivate here while you're pregnant.

Think of the child. You cannot be rash like this. You should have informed them of your condition," Zen admonished.

Margaret nodded at that, humbled. "You're right. I'm sorry." For the first time, Margaret wasn't angered at being admonished. She had rarely gotten angry since she got pregnant.

Zen gently touched Margaret's head and lifted the red chain, removing the Soul Fire Swirl for her.

Then he turned to Letitia. "Eastern Emperor Taiyi summoned me today."

Letitia dropped her eyes. She knew what Zen would say next.

"How could you just decide things on your own like that?" Zen pressed, staring at Letitia.

Letitia lowered her head. "Lady Flamine talked to me. If you marry Elvinia, the Oneness Sky Palace would always be there to help you. It would be good for you. I'll be fine. It makes little difference to me."

Flamine had actually met with Letitia three times. She had been upfront about her purpose and had patiently explained the situation in detail.

Letitia was smart enough to recognize Flamine's painstaking efforts.

She also admired Flamine's honesty.

If Zen became the husband of the Oneness Sky Palace's princess, it would be of great benefit to him. That was why Letitia gave her consent to Flamine.

"I just knew it." Zen sighed. Even before talking to Letitia, he had already guessed she would say something like this.

"So, did you agree to the marriage?" Letitia asked, staring at Zen.

The practical side of her thought was Zen should seize the opportunity. But a part of her was grieving at the thought.

Zen shook his head. "No."

"Why?"

Hearing Zen's answer, Letitia felt relieved and dismayed at the same time.

Honestly, she couldn't understand herself, at times.

"There are just some things that can't and shouldn't be changed," Zen said firmly.

A faint smile appeared on Letitia's face. At this moment, she exuded a kind of quiet charm. A split second later, however, she gave Zen a sly look. "Do you like Elvinia?"

Letitia didn't know Elvinia that much, unlike Lavender, Laquisha, and Nelly who constantly interacted with Elvinia and even regarded her as their master.

"I also want to know the answer."

A faint voice came from the entrance of the Fire Bearing Hall. It was Elvinia.

Chapter 3574 A Conspiracy Letitia fixed Zen with a look.

Margaret looked up at the newly arrived Elvinia as she placed a hand instinctively on her belly.

The old Margaret would have already shown some hostility to Elvinia, jealous of any woman who got close to Zen.

But now she was pregnant, she kept a level head. It hadn't been easy to bear this child. She didn't want her emotions to fluctuate too much and endanger the pregnancy.

Elvinia's face was surprisingly calm, but there was stubbornness in her delicate eyes.

Zen's reaction at the Supreme Dragon Hall to their proposed marriage had subjected Elvinia to embarrassment, but she didn't care. The only thing she wanted to know now was how Zen really felt about her.

Elvinia's lips trembled as she struggled to keep her chin up. She admitted she had a rough relationship with Zen in the beginning, but since their journey to the Dark Region, she had been infatuated with the sense of security she had when she was with him.

She also knew that Zen trusted Dorothy more than her, so she had to be aggressive in making her feelings known.

Zen turned to Elvinia. "Even if I like you, it doesn't mean that you can do this to Tia, manipulating her into doing what you want."

This caused a small smile to play on Letitia's lips. Despite it all, she had still hoped she was the most special one in Zen's heart.

Meanwhile, Margaret pursed her lips. That was just like Zen to say that.

This was why she had spent almost a lifetime at odds with Letitia.

Elvinia, meanwhile, was just happy she finally got her answer. The nervous look in her eyes was replaced almost immediately by relief. "Alright then. It will not happen again."

Smiling to herself, she swept out of the Fire Bearing Hall.

As Zen puzzled over Elvinia's reaction, Letitia, who was next to him, beamed up at him. "That was amazing diplomacy, darling! You made Princess Elvinia compromise."

"Compromise?" Zen blinked in confusion.

"She got the answer she wanted. The least she could do is compromise,"

Margaret muttered.

Zen walked over to Margaret and gently crouched beside her. "Now, don't be like that. Be mindful of your condition. Anyway, the Fire Bearing Hall is not suitable for you. We need to get you out of here as soon as possible."

Zen turned to look at Letitia. "I know you want me to use the Oneness Sky Palace to revive the Nine Li race, but the situation in the Source World has become extremely complicated."

After his visit to the Pear Hill, Zen had come to realize it was meaningless to simply gather the remaining members of the Nine Li race and just start over with so few of them. He needed to complete a more important mission for the Nine Li race's revival.

After he returned to the Oneness Sky Palace from the Pear Hill, he went to the Land of Sword Grief, so he was not able to explain the situation in detail to Letitia then.

Zen was now keeping her up to speed, but only broadly, as he lectured her intermittently on her recent reckless decisions. Although she was being scolded, Letitia had a faint smile on her face all throughout. Zen's concern for her made her happy deep inside.

Through all this, Lavender, Laquisha, and Nelly had been preoccupied cultivating under the Soul Fire Swirl. Zen thought it best not to interrupt their meditation.

Even before arriving here at the Phoenix Palace, Zen had already planned to bring Letitia and Margaret back to the Flow Sword Sect. All the more he wasn't hurrying to return to the Land of Sword Grief now. He gave Carrie some divine crystals and asked her to go to the Dragon City to buy some prenatal healthcare treatments for Margaret.

When Letitia was pregnant with Geoffrey, Zen hadn't been there for her because he had been preoccupied with things in the Upper World. This time, Zen vowed he would fulfill his responsibility as a father.

In the Vastness Mountain, some important people had gathered behind closed doors of the Mighty Sword Hall.

Natasha, Holden, and the two leaders of the intelligence agency of the Vastness Mountain were waiting on their leader.

Wearing a pair of delicate shoes and her red garments, Natasha paced back and forth, a slight frown marring her features.

On the throne at the top of the Mighty Sword Hall, Gethin sat cross-legged, his eyes closed. He was roaming on the Other Shore.

He opened his eyes shortly. They flashed like lightning on his unreadable face. It was obvious he had returned.

"Emperor Gethin!"

The two leaders of the intelligence agency walked forward and bowed to him.

Gethin stroked his beard and frowned. "They will be making a preemptive strike."

Hearing this, Holden and Natasha exchanged a look.

"A preemptive strike? Under present conditions? Wouldn't that just put us at risk?" Natasha asked pointedly.

Although the Vastness Mountain was one of the top three forces in the Oneness Sky Palace, it was far from being as strong as the Oneness Mountain or the Origin Mountain. Moreover, with Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Yasamin guarding the two mountains, respectively, making a move against them would mean certain death.

Holden nodded in agreement. "A preemptive strike would only put us at a disadvantage."

"Emperor Charm is ready," Gethin pointed out.

The Sun Crow race was adjacent to the territory of the Oneness Sky Palace.

They would be the first to attack in a war.

"There is only the Sun Crow race that will take them on?" Natasha only became more hesitant about the idea.

The Vastness Mountain was turning against the Oneness Sky Palace because of Gethin's personal ambition, and on the other hand, he had also lost his faith in them.

But the Oneness Sky Palace was more established, having accumulated resources and allies for countless years. The Sun Crow race would find it hard to destroy them alone. And if the Vastness Mountain acted rashly and was found to be actually behind this conspiracy, they would be put in a precarious situation.

Gethin stared at the door of the Mighty Sword Hall with a faraway look in his eyes. "Their plan is to trap Eastern Emperor Taiyi and Yasamin on the Other Shore!"

The two strongest forces of the Oneness Sky Palace were Yasamin and Eastern Emperor Taiyi. If they were trapped on the Other Shore, the strength of the Oneness Sky Palace would indeed be greatly diminished.

Natasha nodded slowly as she started to understand the strategy. Her eyes flashed hungrily.

"They have supposedly already begun work on Yasamin, though I don't know if they have succeeded or not," Gethin continued. "But someone's name kept coming up."

"Who?" Natasha asked.

"Zen," Gethin replied.

It was true that Zen was a talented warrior, but he held no threat to the Bearing race.

"Do you want us to kill him?" A trace of excitement lit up Natasha's face.

Things didn't end well the last time they kidnapped Zen and took him to the Vastness Mountain. All the trouble hadn't been worth it. What was worse, the Vastness Mountain actually didn't dare do anything to him.

"We need to capture him alive. Zen seems quite important to them." Even Gethin seemed torn about this. Everyone knew Zen was an outstanding talent, but what was the point of keeping him alive? "That's good enough," Natasha sneered, a glint of malice in her eyes.

On the Origin Mountain, a forest of emerald-green trees surrounded a small lake.

Countless arrays had been engraved around these trees.

All together, they formed the Spirit-shaking Array, which protected the small lake and its immediate surroundings.

It was also fully activated whenever Yasamin entered the Other Shore. It was risky, after all, for a powerful being like her to just leave her physical body behind, which was vulnerable to any attack.

Anyone who crossed the Spirit-shaking Array when it was activated would immediately be killed, except for a select few of the Origin Mountain who were allowed to enter it.

Presently, Dorothy stood outside the forest. She paused for a moment before smoothly entering the threshold.

The Spirit-shaking Array released a rune to cover the surface of Dorothy's body. The surrounding trees flashed with a red light.

The light died down as the rune apparently verified Dorothy's identity and allowed her through.

Chapter 3575 Something Unforeseen In The Origin Mountain Dorothy passed through the forest and walked halfway around the lake before she arrived at the pavilion.

She pushed the door of the pavilion open, only to find a wholly different space greeting her from within.

Countless rays of sword light floated in the air, circling around like a big whirlpool. This was the famous Origin Sword Light.

Among all the disciples in the Origin Mountain, few had the chance to be taught by Yasamin herself. And among these few, Dorothy was the only one who had the right to cultivate the Origin Swordsmanship in this space.

Dorothy went up to the whirlpool formed by the sword light.

Yasamin was floating in the center of this whirlpool. She seemed to be adventuring on the Other Shore.

The moment Dorothy approached, a ray of sword light flew towards her.

She stretched out a hand and gently played with the sword light. A long, melodious sound was immediately transmitted into the big whirlpool.

Yasamin was able to sense this on the Other Shore.

If someone else were to play the sword light in an attempt to wake Yasamin, she would have become furious. She would then just ignore the sound and stay on the Other Shore.

But every time Dorothy played the sword light, Yasamin retreated from the Other Shore as soon as possible.

Dorothy played the sword light for a while before she sat down, arms around her knees and waiting for her grandmother to wake up. She was also mentally preparing herself to talk to her grandmother, trying to decide what to say to her.

Her grandmother had figured out her affection towards Zen a long time ago and wanted to help her fulfill her wish. That was why Yasamin had had the conflict with Flamine in the Vastness Mountain.

But though Dorothy was passionate, she was extremely reserved when it came to relationships between man and woman. And though Yasamin was anxious for her granddaughter, she could do nothing about it.

At the time, Dorothy had liked traveling with Zen on the Other Shore. She hadn't thought that Elvinia would appear suddenly.

Chaim had reminded her of her love in the Land of Sword Grief. Only then had Dorothy realized that she should strive for her love, just like Elvinia had.

But the question of how to speak euphemistically to her grandmother still remained.

She fought an internal battle for quite a while. When she came to her senses, she found that five minutes had passed, but her grandmother was still floating at the center of the sword light whirlpool.

Dorothy was confused. Even though Yasamin was on the Other Shore, she should have known that Dorothy was coming. But five minutes had passed and she still hadn't retreated from the Other Shore. Could she have been trapped somewhere unusual? There were some places like the Dark Region and the temples that warriors were not allowed to exit at will.

Dorothy was discomfited as she remembered the provocative look in Elvinia's eyes. So she merely waited.

She waited for about one more hour before she realized that there seemed to be something wrong with her grandmother. Yasamin's body seemed somewhat illusory in the midst of the sword light, but Dorothy could still see her clearly.

Yasamin's wrinkled face was usually ruddy, but it was now pale as paper.

"Grandma!"

Dorothy's cultivation level was not very high, but she knew that something was wrong.

She played the sword light once again. The sword light buzzed sharply and was transmitted to within the whirlpool. Her grandmother would wake up the moment she heard this sound, she knew it.

But Yasamin remained motionless. Her face paled with every passing second and every ray of Origin Sword Light in the entire space began to vibrate.

This sword light could be seen as Yasamin's avatar. It would usually be taken back to her body. But when she cultivated here, she'd release all the Origin Sword Light from her body.

Dorothy was familiar with the sword light. It trembled and howled, as if sensing that Yasamin was in danger. It sobbed and complained to Dorothy.

"Grandma! Grandma!"

The scene unfolding before Dorothy reminded her that Yasamin was in trouble.

She took a couple of steps forward before she realized that she couldn't get close to her grandmother. She remembered that every time Yasamin had woken up, she emerged from the whirlpool by herself.

Dorothy thought for a moment before she turned around and rushed out of the pavilion. Emerging from the forest, she pulled out the message runes and crushed them one by one.

Before long, beams of light flew up from the halls in the Origin Mountain.

They headed straight for the top of the mountain, gathering outside the forest.

Each of these had a strong aura. Not for nothing were they the backbone of the Origin Mountain. Winchell, one of the few people qualified to enter the forest, led the group.

At Dorothy's words, he went straight into the forest without hesitation.

Two other people accompanied him into the forest.

Dorothy meant to follow them but the moment she took a step forward, she felt her foot become heavy.

It looked like even a powerful existence like her grandmother, who was at the top level of the Other Shore Realm, couldn't avoid danger.

She was afraid that once she entered the forest, she would see her grandmother's soulless body before her.

She trembled with fear at the thought, but someone caught her from behind.

"Aunt Felicity!" Dorothy cried out.

"Don't be afraid. Everything will be fine," Felicity said, comforting her while looking at the forest. "Madam Yasamin will safely leave the Other Shore."

It would actually be very difficult for a warrior at such a high level as Yasamin to die on the Other Shore, because the souls of strongest warriors like them had already risen to another level.

'So, did something unexpected happen on the Other Shore?' Felicity had many possibilities mapped out in her mind, but she did not say anything. She merely tried to comfort Dorothy in a soft voice.

After a long time, Winchell walked out of the forest.

Dorothy felt her heart plummet at the seriousness on his face. She then heard him say, "I think Madam Yasamin is trapped in a dangerous situation, but she is still fighting hard. I don't know how long she can hold on. I'm going to the Phoenix Palace."

The seven mountains under the Oneness Sky Palace were closely connected to each other, like siblings. And especially the Oneness Mountain and the Origin Mountain. Now that something terrible was happening to Yasamin, they had to inform Eastern Emperor Taiyi as soon as possible.

With gloom dangling over them, Felicity, Dorothy, and the other powerful warriors of the Origin Mountain watched Winchell leave.

In the Flow Sword Sect...

Margaret had been very satisfied over the past few days. Zen had been with her all the time, and even Letitia had taken good care of her. The atmosphere in the independent courtyard house had never been so harmonious.

Letitia had once suggested that Margaret enter Zen's inner world. If the time flow rate rose, she would be able to give birth to the baby sooner. But Margaret refused because she didn't want her pregnancy to pass quickly.

"A Fetus Nourishing Pill, worth two million divine crystals, can nourish the innate spirit!"

"An Earth Longevity Pill, worth five hundred thousand divine crystals, can help you live for a million years even if you don't cultivate or become a True God!"

"A Talent Upgrading Pill, worth five million divine crystals, can help you improve your cultivation talent greatly!"

...

Trish displayed before Zen the pills that she had bought.

Zen could not help but feel amazed after learning of the effects of these pills. It looked like the starting point in the Source World was much higher than in the divine land. And these pills had little to no side effects when used to nourish the fetus.

Chapter 3576 Three Thousand And One Godly Ways With the current resources Zen possessed, the cost of tens of millions of divine crystals wouldn't be an issue. He was capable of producing the Sword-reading Liquid, which was highly valuable. As such, he had made a batch before he returned to the Flow Sword Sect.

As for the earnings, Zen had requested Monica to distribute the divine crystals to the Sword Light Palace disciples instead of keeping them for himself.

After all, Zen had Stage Fourteen to back him. The place had a massive amount of wealth. The number of divine crystals he gave to these disciples was nothing to him.

Margaret didn't have the easiest time refining the nourishing pills that her baby needed. However, with Trish's guidance, she showed exceptional tenacity and was able to focus a full week on refining all the pills using complicated methods.

During the past few days, apart from taking care of Margaret and accompanying Letitia and Aura, Zen also visited the neighboring courtyard house.

Hutton, Sally, and the other Nine Li members waited for Ambrose to pick them up after they returned to the Oneness Sky Palace. However, Ambrose never arrived. They never mentioned anything about leaving, either.

The tiny kingdom belonging to the remaining members of the Nine Li race couldn't hold a candle to the majesty of the Oneness Sky Palace. Luckily, Despite that they were unable to enter the Land of Sword Grief, Zen was able to provide them with the required resources in the Myriad Spirits City.

Thanks to his help, they made rapid progress.

If Sally could get into the Land of Sword Grief, she could attain a rank within the top nine hundred on the first floor.

Soon after he returned to his own courtyard house after the visit, a strange sensation passed throughout Zen's body. With a slight frown, he sat crosslegged on the floor. With a slight thought in his mind, an avatar had appeared within his inner world.

Even with the removal of the Evil God's Rebirth Land, everything within it remained.

Ever since the Evil God was brought back to Zen's inner world, he had been imprisoned together with his wife, Edna.

She proved her loyalty well, choosing to stay at his side despite her imprisonment.

This time, when the Evil God returned, Edna noticed he seemed depressed.

He talked less than usual, barely uttering a single word to her. She also noticed how he was lost in thought as if thinking of something profound.

All of this worried her.

She knew that her husband would never compromise or give up. He was as stubborn as a bull, never wanting to give up a chance to turn the tables— unless he was destroyed.

The Creator of the world the Evil God and Edna were imprisoned in was an omnipotent being—all that existed in his inner world was essentially a part of him. If the Evil God even just thought about rebelling, the Creator would know immediately.

Edna herself never dared to give any thought to the idea, afraid that if the Creator found out, he would be more wary of her husband.

If there was anything she was thankful for, it was that the Creator gave her husband the Blood Essence Godly Way. Ever since then, he'd been fully immersed in fusing the Godly Ways. It relieved her knowing that he had found something he was interested in.

The Evil God had offered the Creator his Rebirth Land, and even a "Civilization Artifact"—which Edna, although not knowing much about it, knew that it possessed terrifying and threatening energy. In fact, the power it contained would be countless times more terrifying than that of the Waysblending Energy her husband had.

If her husband could manage to find a way to seamlessly merge the Blood Essence Godly Way into the Ways-blending Energy, then he'd receive atonement for his sins and get the opportunity to roam freely in this world.

Perhaps then, she and he could return to their old happy days.

Lost deep in thought, Edna was startled back to reality by the sudden flash of lightning.

The Evil God held a ball of great power in his right hand. It was the Waysblending Energy, a power comprised of two thousand nine hundred and ninety-eight Godly Ways. His left hand wielded the Thunderstorm Godly Way which startled her earlier.

He gently opened his left hand, and with a cracking sound, the Thunderstorm Godly Way had shot into the Ways-blending Energy. The Evil God was happy to see it still remain stable.

"Buzz!"

With the wave of his left hand, a streak of small, blood-red energy spiraled around his fingers and turned into a blood-red dragon.

There was no denying that the Evil God had an extraordinary understanding of the various Godly Ways. After Zen got the Blood Essence Godly Way, he didn't pursue practicing it. As for the Evil God, he now actually could use it with such ease and at a super level.

The blood-red dragon twined through his fingertips until it made its way to the ball of Ways-blending Energy. By then, the ball already had three thousand kinds of internal momentum within it! The Evil God had previously tried to combine the arc light energy with the other Godly Ways in order to reach three thousand Godly Ways in the Ways-blending Energy. However, it clashed with the Thunderstorm Godly Way. So he began his long journey of trying various ways to combine but there was always a Godly Way that was rejected.

Now, the Evil God was successful. He managed to replace the arc light energy with the Blood Essence Godly Way.

"I did it!"

The Evil God finally managed to smile after all this time as he gazed at his success in his hands—the ball of energy really had three thousand Godly Ways in it. It had been a while since he felt this happy.

If it was before, the Evil God would have thought that he had finally achieved the Godly Ways Great Unity.

But he already knew that there were more than three thousand types of internal momentum—around three thousand and two according to Zen. So, even if it reached three thousand, that still wouldn't be enough for him to achieve the Godly Ways Great Unity.

After successfully merging the Blood Essence Godly Way with others, his fingertips now flashed with the arc light energy which he shot towards the Ways-blending Energy he still held in his other hand.

Once the arc light energy disappeared, the Ways-blending Energy began to alter once more. Unfortunately, it became unstable, and more than thirty Godly Ways escaped the powerful orb.

"How can this be? I…I did everything right…"

The Evil God was slightly shocked. He only hesitated for a moment. Seeing that the Ways-blending Energy was about to explode, he flicked his left hand and merged the more than thirty Godly Ways separately into a ball and then merge them with the Ways-blending Energy again.

"Buzz..."

The Ways-blending Energy became stable once more. The fusion of the internal momentum of three thousand and one Godly Ways was successful.

"It appears that fusing the more than 30 kinds of internal momentum that have escaped is what's required to stabilize the Ways-blending Energy and succeed." The Evil God muttered as a wave of relief washed over him.

Such a creation of power wouldn't have been possible without the extraordinary talent showcased by the Evil God. Any other person who dared to re-enact what he just accomplished would have to explore for tens or even hundreds of thousands of years.

Once three thousand and one Godly Ways were fused together, the Waysblending Energy morphed once more into a bright, purple-tinged light.

"Darling, the power seems to keep getting stronger!" Edna exclaimed as she drew near to her husband's side.

"Yes!"

The Evil God nodded, a smile of satisfaction plastered on his face. With each gentle wave of his hands, the Ways-blending Energy continued to shift into the shape of diamond. Then it began to overlap itself.

In the blink of an eye, the Evil God had made the diamond-shaped energy superimpose into nearly one hundred layers! "Go!"

The Evil God flicked his fingers, and the diamond-shaped energy shot forward.

Bang! Suddenly, the diamond shaped-energy exploded and emitted a blazing white light that shone as bright as the sun with hints of purple-tinged streams scattered throughout.

Edna quickly covered her eyes and hid behind her husband. The Evil God, on the other hand, gazed at it head-on in excitement.

The power of Evil God's Ways-blending Energy had reached beyond ten thousand divine megatons. This surpassed his expectations.

He knew that with his current limits, he could enable the Ways-blending Energy to have up to one hundred and ninety-three layers. If this was the power that one hundred layers could achieve, surely nothing could stop him once he reached his limit.

Using all of his strength would enable the power to double itself! The light emitted by the Ways-blending Energy shot in all directions. Just as it was about to wreak havoc in Zen's inner world, the light suddenly froze before shrinking back once more into its original diamond-shaped state. It was as if someone had forced the hands of the clock backward.

Zen appeared beside the diamond-shaped energy and gently reached out to take the ball of energy in his hand, watching it thoughtfully.

Chapter 3577 Reward Zen was thoroughly alarmed the moment the Evil God had succeeded in completely blending the Godly Ways.

The power within the diamond-shaped energy greatly exceeded the expectations of the Evil God. It was also way beyond Zen could have ever imagined.

As the diamond-shaped energy exploded, it released a huge amount of energy that transcended ten thousand divine megatons of force. Without a doubt, Zen thought he probably wouldn't have been able to withstand this extreme amount of force if it had happened outside his inner world.

Thankfully, this didn't pose much of a problem inside Zen's inner world.

Here, he was an omnipotent being. He was the absolute ruler of this place and his power was unparalleled. Therefore, he could easily restore everything in their original forms.

The Evil God had intended this enormous amount of energy to explode completely. He wanted to observe and ascertain its full might.

However, Zen halted his experiment midway. He was annoyed and frowned at the sudden interruption.

Zen didn't have to raise his head and look at the Evil God for he knew that there was a change in his emotions. He felt the annoyance and bitterness the Evil God felt. "I'm afraid this huge amount of power would obliterate more than half of my inner world if it completely explodes. You have to understand why I stopped it," he explained.

"Oh, is that it? So you also have something to be afraid of, huh?" The Evil God sneered at Zen's remark. He still couldn't keep the annoyance out of his tone.

Zen held the diamond-shaped energy on his palm as he slowly flew over to where the Evil God was. "Well theoretically, there shouldn't be anything that could make me afraid in my own inner world. However, your presence is an exception."

Essentially, the creation of the Evil God took up some of Zen's best talents.

There were always pros and cons to his existence. If the Evil God stayed inside Zen's inner world, then as a primitive land, it would go through many tribulations. These ordeals also served as great trials for Zen.

Zen hovered in front of the golden fence and handed the diamond-shaped energy to the Evil God. "You did a great job." He faced the Evil God and praised him sincerely. He had to admit that he was impressed at this display of power.

"It didn't do me any good, though, did it?" The Evil God seemed dejected as he scowled at Zen.

"Yes, it did. For that, I will give you a handsome reward," replied Zen.

Nevertheless, the Evil God wasn't surprised by Zen's words. He also didn't seem interested in it.

Zen had once set the Evil God free after he helped him blend the many Godly Ways. However, he believed that Zen wouldn't make the mistake of doing that again after his open betrayal of him. He desired nothing else but his freedom. Therefore, he showed absolutely no interest in Zen's so-called reward.

"Would you kindly repeat the process of blending the Godly Ways to me?"

Zen asked courteously.

From inside the fence, the Evil God merely glanced sideways at Zen as he disintegrated the diamond-shaped energy in his hand. He couldn't be bothered to repeat the whole process in front of Zen.

"My dear, the Creator himself demands this from you. So please, just do it again," coaxed Edna who was standing behind the Evil God. She never thought it was a wise move to go against the will of their creator.

"He doesn't really need me to do it again. He is able to get the knowledge by himself," retorted the Evil God coldly.

The corners of Zen's mouth curled into a smile. He reached out in front of him and clenched his fist. A long sword instantly appeared in his hand. He conjured it out of thin air.

Normally, a sword created in such a casual way was fragile and of poor quality. However, this was Zen's inner world. Therefore, he was able to improve and enhance it to the highest level with just a single thought.

He remained motionless with the sword in his hand for a short time. Several visions playing one after another flashed in front of his eyes.

In Zen's mind, the scene of the Evil God blending the Godly Ways began to unfold. Impressively, it didn't leave out any details at all! Buzz! The Ways-blending Energy began to gather around the long sword in Zen's hand. Two thousand nine hundred and ninety-nine kinds of internal momentum assembled first. These were followed by the Thunderstorm Godly Way and the Blood Essence Godly Way. The arc light energy came in last! Whoosh! After Zen blended them in order, he encountered the same accident that the Evil God had experienced a while ago. There were more than thirty kinds of internal momentum of the Godly Ways that automatically split from the others.

Zen had already observed this odd occurrence so he was well prepared for it. With a flick of his hand, these more than thirty Godly Ways formed into a mass of energy and merged into the Ways-blending Energy.

There was a flash of purple light that emanated from it. This signaled that Zen was successful in blending all of them together.

As Zen held the sword in his hand, he said, "I don't have any spare time to cultivate the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship. Fortunately, it is much similar to the diamond-shaped energy you have created. Therefore, I can just learn from your experience of creating this energy!"

Zen had to admit that he was a bit envious of the Evil God's sheer talent of blending the Godly Ways.

The Evil God was able to create this method almost instinctively. Even though the diamond-shaped energy he created was not a specific skill, it still had a much greater stability and comprehensibility than the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship written by Eastern Emperor Taiyi.

It was extremely noteworthy that it took Eastern Emperor Taiyi a lot of time and energy to complete the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship. This was regarded far and wide as a supreme swordsmanship manual. Compared to that, it was only a short span of time from when the Evil God had first grasped the Ways-blending Energy.

It was true that there were times when Zen had felt the urge to devour the Evil God and take his talent as his own. However, he would immediately pull himself together as he thought of the Regal Jade Spirit's warning.

Suddenly, there was a clanging sound.

Three gleams of purple sword radiance merged together. Zen summoned them according to the methods of the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship. But during the course of it, Zen made some changes and turned the sword radiance into diamond-shaped energy. He used the method he had just learned from the Evil God while he blended them.

When Zen returned the Evil God to his inner world, he gathered all of the Evil God's Other Shore Tokens and everything else that belonged to him.

These included his memories and experiences as well.

However, Zen did not pry into the Evil God's memories out of respect. He only acquired his knowledge of blending the diamond-shaped energy.

Ten layers...

Fifty layers...

One hundred...

One hundred and ninety...

As the number of the energy layers gathering on the sword increased, the Ways-blending Energy also became increasingly formidable.

Soon enough, the Ways-blending Energy on the long sword became so intimidating that even the Evil God gasped in astonishment. "This energy will be unbelievably powerful when used in swordsmanship," he remarked.

"Eastern Emperor Taiyi is one of the most powerful masters in the Source World. His strength is comparable to that of the Black Ship's captain. It can be expected that the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship he wrote has its merits. If you are interested to read it, I can get it for you," offered Zen.

As mentioned before, the Godly Ways Blending Swordsmanship was regarded as a supreme swordsmanship manual. Therefore, it was not allowed to be handed down to outsiders. However, Zen could lend it to the Evil God if he wanted.

As he finished saying this, Zen suddenly raised his hand that held the sword.

The sword slashed and pierced the air at the distance. The purple sword radiance contained almost twenty thousand divine megatons of force. As it erupted forth, the space in its path was shattered into pieces.

But before the sword radiance had completely exploded, Zen created a huge black rift in space using his mind. It appeared in front of the sword radiance and swallowed it whole.

He could not allow the sword radiance to explode inside his inner world. It was powerful enough to obliterate the entirety of this world.

"What's the point of learning this swordsmanship if I cannot leave your inner world? It will only be a waste of time and talent." The Evil God hung his head and replied sourly.

Zen fixed his gaze at the Evil God. "Well, I agree. It will be such an awful waste to keep you imprisoned inside my inner world."

As he heard these words, the Evil God instantly raised his head. He stared confusedly at Zen and wondered whether he was telling the truth.

Zen reached out his hand toward the Evil God and offered him a handful of Chaotic Source Spirits. Then, he said, "Here's two hundred Chaotic Source Spirits. These will be enough for you to reach the Chaotic Source Realm."

The Evil God was fully aware of the Chaotic Source Spirit's absolute importance because he had once been sent into the Chaotic Source World by the Black Ship. However, he had given up hope of ever reaching the Chaotic Source Realm after his rebellion against Zen failed. Never in his wildest dreams had he expected that Zen would freely hand him such a gift.

Zen knew that the Evil God would plainly refuse any other kind of reward.

However, if he offered him Chaotic Source Spirits...

The Evil God took them from Zen without any second thoughts.

Chapter 3578 Release In the future, the Chaotic Source World would no longer exist, and thus there would be no way to obtain the Chaotic Source Spirits. This was probably the last chance for the Evil God to step into the Chaotic Source Realm.

"You need to arrange an array to refine the crystals of Chaotic Source Spirits. I'll help you get the array arrangement method later," Zen added.

His tone was steady, as if he was confident despite the worrying situation he was in.

After the Chaotic Source Spirits had been successfully placed into his body, the Evil God needed a magic array to refine them.

This place was too far away from the abandoned Chaotic Source World. It was impossible for Zen to let the Evil God go there to refine the Chaotic Source Spirits. Besides, Zen thought the array used to refine them shouldn't be difficult to arrange. He would find an opportunity to inquire about it to make sure before he acted.

"What do you mean by that?" the Evil God asked. Curiosity gleamed in his eyes as he spoke.

Indeed, he was interested in the crystals of Chaotic Source Spirits.

However, he was more interested in what Zen had just said.

A smile appeared in Zen's eyes.

The Evil God was indeed unwilling to be trapped in his inner world.

"I want to let you out," said Zen calmly.

"Let me out?" The eyes of the Evil God flickered. His brows were crossed and his glare was steady. It was hard to believe what he had heard and he couldn't hide the surprise and excitement he felt after hearing what Zen said.

Ever since he was caught by Zen, the Evil God had been desperate and uneasy as he waited for Zen to devour him.

Yet, unexpectedly, Zen didn't do that. Instead, he just imprisoned him and let him study the Ways-blending Energy. However, with his intelligence, he knew just why Zen did this.

Just as Zen had said before, if he really was the malice of this world, absorbing him would only bring greater trouble to Zen.

Zen had let him go before, but at that time, he had used the Rebirth Land to bind him.

However, Zen had already discovered the defects of the Rebirth Land, and because of this, he wouldn't use it again.

Just as the Evil God was thinking, Zen spoke, "There's only one condition.

You'll have to become my Inner-world Generating Avatar."

Before entering the Chaotic Source World, the Evil God had learned about the Inner-world Generating Avatar. It was a method of refining the creatures in one's inner world into avatars.

Previously, the Evil God also wanted to refine Zen into his own avatar. If he could possess a powerful body like Zen's, then he would be even more powerful.

To his surprise, the final result was the opposite.

Zen continued, "However, the ordinary Inner-world Generating Avatar has no consciousness and serves as the avatar of its owner, but I plan to let you keep your consciousness. In other words, you have freedom in most cases, but you can't disobey my orders."

After returning to the Oneness Sky Palace, Zen spared some time learning about the Inner-world Generating Avatar. It was not a complicated theurgy.

He could directly control the avatar in this way, so it was more practical than the Rebirth Land.

Refining the Evil God into an ordinary avatar wouldn't be of much use to Zen. In fact, when it came to physical strength, the Evil God was far inferior to him. But the Evil God was more talented than him in some aspects. Zen thought that if he could use the Evil God's talents properly, it would be a great help to him.

After explaining, Zen straightened his body and cleared his throat to ask, "Are you willing to do that?"

"Well, it looks like I have no choice," the Evil God said with a smile.

Deep down, the Evil God was willing to do what Zen offered. No matter what, Zen's offer was much better than being trapped in his inner world.

Moreover, he thought that the Inner-world Generating Avatar might not be...

As the Evil God was about to be absorbed in his thought, he stopped and realized something. Since Zen was able to read his mind, he couldn't think of some things.

Zen took a few steps forward and waved his hand at the golden fence. The whole fence broke, and the mountain collapsed with a loud thud.

When the mortals in the kingdoms below saw the mountain collapse, they all panicked in fear. There were shrieks and sounds of the people's feet in stampede.

"Creator, I..." Edna floated in the air and looked at Zen with a pleading expression.

There were many living beings in the inner world, but they weren't aware that there was a big world outside, so naturally, they didn't have too many thoughts in their hearts.

Once they knew about the outside world, they wouldn't be willing to be confined in this world.

As the Evil God's wife, Edna had known for a long time that there existed a big world outside. However, rather than visit that big world, she was more willing to follow the Evil God.

"You can leave with him. I don't have any restrictions for you," Zen said directly.

The expression on Edna's face changed and she immediately cheered, "Thank you, Creator!"

Even the Evil God was quite surprised, and there was a trace of joy in his eyes that he hadn't had for a long time.

Then, with Zen's permission, the Evil God and Edna went to the main continent to say goodbye to their children.

Although the Evil God had left for a long time, he already became a legend in Zen's inner world. Many secrets of this world were controlled by his children. Even without his presence, his children still turned out to be outstanding in this world.

When his children saw that he had returned, they couldn't hide their surprise. When they heard that their father and mother were going to leave together, they were wistful. However, as the children of the Evil God, they understood his pursuit.

After Zen dissipated his incarnation, he regained his consciousness. The moment he opened his eyes, he felt a warm breath on his face. Then he saw Margaret's face was very close to him.

"What are you doing?" Zen asked, dumbfounded. He blinked his eyes rapidly and crossed his brows.

Glaring at Zen, Margaret said, "I saw you meditating in the yard. I was afraid that something might happen to you..."

She thought Zen had gone to the Other Shore.

Letitia, Lavender and the other women had a certain understanding of the Other Shore, but Margaret was completely unable to understand it. In all honesty, she had no interest in understanding it. She only knew that the Other Shore was very dangerous.

Zen touched Margaret's head and comforted her in a soft voice, "I just went to my inner world."

"Why did you go there?" She leaned in towards him, obviously wanting to hear more details. Curiosity was reflecting in her eyes as she waited for his response.

"Someone is coming out," Zen answered Margaret simply.

At his words, Zen stood up and circled around. He stopped in an empty place and led his hands to the air from his abdomen. Then, Edna in white appeared in the courtyard.

It was the first time for Edna to come to this world. She looked terrified and curious at the same time.

"Creator, do you live in this place?" Edna asked.

In her eyes, Zen was an all-powerful and invincible god. Although this independent courtyard house was truly exquisite, it was very ordinary and too low for Zen. This mundane environment confused her.

"Zen, who is she?"

A moment ago, Margaret was as docile as a sheep, but as Edna appeared, her face darkened, as if she was about to lose her temper.

"She is from my inner world. I promised to release her," Zen explained.

"Just because she is beautiful?" Margaret complained. Her brows were raised and her tone was probing. Margaret narrowed her eyes and gave Edna a look from her head to toe.

Edna, as the Evil God's wife, was exceedingly beautiful. Margaret felt a great sense of crisis in her heart. In fact, Letitia was looking down from the second floor. Not far away, Trish, Carrie and Aura were secretly sizing Edna up.
